

######################################
###   Guangdong Scripted Effects   ###
######################################

#Updates the Guangdong status dynamic modifier as well as swapping out its corresponding dummy event.
#Set the Guangdong status variable (GNG_general_status_var) to your desired value first, then run the command.
#1 - Between Two Worlds
#2 - Yasuda Crisis
#3 - Silicon Years
#4 - Guangdong Riots
#5 - State
#6 - Corporate, Matsushita
#7 - Corporate, Ibuka
#8 - Hitachi, Go back to Manchuria Nissan boy (best path - willm)
#9 - IJA OH GOD OH FUCK OH GOD OH FUCK
#10 - :withered:
GNG_update_status = {
	set_variable = { GNG_general_status_var = GNG_general_status_var_temp }
	hidden_effect = {
		remove_ideas = {
			GNG_between_two_worlds_dummy
			GNG_yasuda_crisis_dummy
			GNG_silicon_years_dummy
			GNG_oil_crisis_dummy
			GNG_guangdong_riots_dummy
			GNG_state_path_dummy
			GNG_matsushita_path_dummy
			GNG_ibuka_path_dummy
			GNG_hitachi_path_dummy
			GNG_IJA_path_martial_law_dummy
			GNG_IJA_path_south_china_area_army_dummy
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					GNG_general_status_var = 10
				}
			}
			add_ideas = GNG_IJA_path_south_china_area_army_dummy
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_construction_speed = -1 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_factory_output = -1 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_gdp_growth = -7 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_rgdp = -7 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_stab = -1 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_warsup = -1 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_pp = -0.3 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_republic_of_china_cap = 0.0 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_japanese_empire_cap = 0.0 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_misc_income_modifier = 0.00 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_misc_costs_modifier = 0.0 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_social_costs_modifier = 0.0 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_military_costs_modifier = 0.00 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_admin_costs_modifier = 0.0 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_product_profitability_modifier = 0.0 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_product_seats_modifier = 0.0 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_misc_costs_percent_of_GDP_modifier = 0.00 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					GNG_general_status_var = 9
				}
			}
			add_ideas = GNG_IJA_path_martial_law_dummy
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_construction_speed = -0.3 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_factory_output = -0.3 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_gdp_growth = -5 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_rgdp = -5 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_stab = -1 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_warsup = -1 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_pp = -0.4 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_republic_of_china_cap = 0.0 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_japanese_empire_cap = 0.0 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_misc_income_modifier = 0.00 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_misc_costs_modifier = 0.0 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_social_costs_modifier = 0.0 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_military_costs_modifier = 0.00 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_admin_costs_modifier = 0.0 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_product_profitability_modifier = 0.0 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_product_seats_modifier = 0.0 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_misc_costs_percent_of_GDP_modifier = 0.00 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					GNG_general_status_var = 8
				}
			}
			add_ideas = GNG_hitachi_path_dummy
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_construction_speed = -0.1 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_factory_output = 0.2 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_gdp_growth = -0.50 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_rgdp = 2 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_stab = 0.2 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_warsup = -0.1 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_pp = 0.2 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_product_profitability_modifier = 0 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_product_seats_modifier = 0 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_misc_costs_percent_of_GDP_modifier = 0 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					GNG_general_status_var = 7
				}
			}
			add_ideas = GNG_ibuka_path_dummy
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_construction_speed = 0 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_factory_output = 0.15 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_gdp_growth = 0.00 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_rgdp = 1.5 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_stab = 0.15 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_warsup = 0.00 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_pp = 0.15 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_product_profitability_modifier = 0 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_product_seats_modifier = 0 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_misc_costs_percent_of_GDP_modifier = 0 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					GNG_general_status_var = 6
				}
			}
			add_ideas = GNG_matsushita_path_dummy
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_construction_speed = 0.1 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_factory_output = 0.05 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_gdp_growth = 0.3 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_rgdp = 0.3 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_stab = 0.10 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_warsup = 0.05 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_pp = 0.15 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_product_profitability_modifier = 0 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_product_seats_modifier = 0 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_misc_costs_percent_of_GDP_modifier = 0 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					GNG_general_status_var = 5
				}
			}
			add_ideas = GNG_state_path_dummy
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_construction_speed = 0.2 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_factory_output = 0 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_gdp_growth = 1.5 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_rgdp = 0 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_stab = 0.05 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_warsup = 0.15 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_pp = 0.1 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_product_profitability_modifier = 0 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_product_seats_modifier = 0 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_misc_costs_percent_of_GDP_modifier = 0 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					GNG_general_status_var = 4
				}
			}
			add_ideas = GNG_guangdong_riots_dummy
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_construction_speed = -0.3 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_factory_output = -0.3 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_stab = -0.5 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_warsup = -0.5 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_pp = -0.15 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_misc_costs_percent_of_GDP_modifier = 0.025 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					GNG_general_status_var = 3
				}
			}
			add_ideas = GNG_oil_crisis_dummy
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_construction_speed = -0.5 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_factory_output = -0.5 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_gdp_growth = -3.5 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_rgdp = -5 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_stab = -0.35 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_warsup = -0.35 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_pp = -0.4 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_product_profitability_modifier = -0.5 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_product_seats_modifier = -0.5 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_misc_costs_percent_of_GDP_modifier = 0.075 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					GNG_general_status_var = 2
				}
			}
			add_ideas = GNG_silicon_years_dummy
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_stab = -0.15 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_warsup = -0.15 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_pp = -0.05 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_rgdp = -1.0 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_gdp_growth = 1.5 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					GNG_general_status_var = 1
				}
			}
			add_ideas = GNG_yasuda_crisis_dummy
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_stab = -0.3 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_warsup = -0.3 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_pp = -0.2 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_rgdp = -2.5 }
		}
		else = {
			add_ideas = GNG_between_two_worlds_dummy
		}
	}
	force_update_dynamic_modifier = yes
	add_to_variable = { GNG_map_dirty_variable = 0.01 }
	add_to_variable = { GNG_product_decisions_dirty_variable = 0.01 }
	add_to_variable = { GNG_3E_dirty_variable = 0.01 }
	add_to_variable = { GNG_economy_dirty_variable = 0.01 }
	custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_update_general_status_tt
}

GNG_update_corruption = {
	set_variable = { GNG_corruption_status_var = GNG_corruption_status_var_temp }
	hidden_effect = {
		remove_ideas = {
			GNG_corruption_the_finest_money_can_buy_dummy
			GNG_corruption_corrupt_dummy
			GNG_corruption_passable_dummy
			GNG_corruption_asias_finest_dummy
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					GNG_corruption_status_var = 3
				}
			}
			add_ideas = GNG_corruption_asias_finest_dummy
			set_variable = { GNG_corruption_monthly_corruption = 0.3 }
			set_variable = { GNG_corruption_republic_of_china_support_cap = 0 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					GNG_corruption_status_var = 2
				}
			}
			add_ideas = GNG_corruption_passable_dummy
			set_variable = { GNG_corruption_monthly_corruption = 0.5 }
			set_variable = { GNG_corruption_republic_of_china_support_cap = -2.5 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					GNG_corruption_status_var = 1
				}
			}
			add_ideas = GNG_corruption_corrupt_dummy
			set_variable = { GNG_corruption_monthly_corruption = 0.7 }
			set_variable = { GNG_corruption_republic_of_china_support_cap = -3.75 }
		}
		else = {
			add_ideas = GNG_corruption_the_finest_money_can_buy_dummy
			set_variable = { GNG_corruption_monthly_corruption = 0.9 }
			set_variable = { GNG_corruption_republic_of_china_support_cap = -5 }
		}
	}
	force_update_dynamic_modifier = yes
	add_to_variable = { GNG_map_dirty_variable = 0.01 }
	add_to_variable = { GNG_product_decisions_dirty_variable = 0.01 }
	add_to_variable = { GNG_3E_dirty_variable = 0.01 }
	add_to_variable = { GNG_economy_dirty_variable = 0.01 }
	custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_update_corruption_status_tt
}

GNG_improve_corruption = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = GNG_corruption_the_finest_money_can_buy_dummy
		}
		set_temp_variable = { GNG_corruption_status_var_temp = 1 }
		GNG_update_corruption = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = GNG_corruption_corrupt_dummy
		}
		set_temp_variable = { GNG_corruption_status_var_temp = 2 }
		GNG_update_corruption = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = GNG_corruption_passable_dummy
		}
		set_temp_variable = { GNG_corruption_status_var_temp = 3 }
		GNG_update_corruption = yes
	}
}

GNG_update_fiscal = {
	set_variable = { GNG_fiscal_status_var = GNG_fiscal_status_var_temp }
	hidden_effect = {
		remove_ideas = {
			GNG_fiscal_sound_dummy
			GNG_fiscal_caution_dummy
			GNG_fiscal_warning_dummy
			GNG_fiscal_problematic_dummy
			GNG_fiscal_emergency_dummy
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					GNG_fiscal_status_var = 4
				}
			}
			add_ideas = GNG_fiscal_emergency_dummy
			set_variable = { GNG_fiscal_inflation_rate = 0.3 }
			set_variable = { GNG_fiscal_pp_gain = -0.15 }
			set_variable = { GNG_fiscal_credit_rating = 3 }
			set_temp_variable = { temp_credit_rating = 3 }
			set_temp_variable = { temp_credit_rating_min = 3 }
			set_temp_variable = { temp_credit_rating_max = 3 }
			econ_initialize_credit_rating_system = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					GNG_fiscal_status_var = 3
				}
			}
			add_ideas = GNG_fiscal_problematic_dummy
			set_variable = { GNG_fiscal_inflation_rate = 0.45 }
			set_variable = { GNG_fiscal_pp_gain = -0.05 }
			set_variable = { GNG_fiscal_credit_rating = 5 }
			set_temp_variable = { temp_credit_rating = 5 }
			set_temp_variable = { temp_credit_rating_min = 5 }
			set_temp_variable = { temp_credit_rating_max = 5 }
			econ_initialize_credit_rating_system = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					GNG_fiscal_status_var = 2
				}
			}
			add_ideas = GNG_fiscal_warning_dummy
			set_variable = { GNG_fiscal_inflation_rate = 0.2 }
			set_variable = { GNG_fiscal_pp_gain = 0. }
			set_variable = { GNG_fiscal_credit_rating = 6 }
			set_temp_variable = { temp_credit_rating = 6 }
			set_temp_variable = { temp_credit_rating_min = 6 }
			set_temp_variable = { temp_credit_rating_max = 6 }
			econ_initialize_credit_rating_system = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					GNG_fiscal_status_var = 1
				}
			}
			add_ideas = GNG_fiscal_caution_dummy
			set_variable = { GNG_fiscal_inflation_rate = -0.05 }
			set_variable = { GNG_fiscal_pp_gain = 0.05 }
			set_variable = { GNG_fiscal_credit_rating = 7 }
			set_temp_variable = { temp_credit_rating = 7 }
			set_temp_variable = { temp_credit_rating_min = 7 }
			set_temp_variable = { temp_credit_rating_max = 7 }
			econ_initialize_credit_rating_system = yes
		}
		else = {
			add_ideas = GNG_fiscal_sound_dummy
			set_variable = { GNG_fiscal_inflation_rate = -0.25 }
			set_variable = { GNG_fiscal_pp_gain = 0.15 }
			set_variable = { GNG_fiscal_credit_rating = 8 }
			set_temp_variable = { temp_credit_rating = 8 }
			set_temp_variable = { temp_credit_rating_min = 8 }
			set_temp_variable = { temp_credit_rating_max = 8 }
			econ_initialize_credit_rating_system = yes
		}
	}
	force_update_dynamic_modifier = yes
	add_to_variable = { GNG_map_dirty_variable = 0.01 }
	add_to_variable = { GNG_product_decisions_dirty_variable = 0.01 }
	add_to_variable = { GNG_3E_dirty_variable = 0.01 }
	add_to_variable = { GNG_economy_dirty_variable = 0.01 }
}

GNG_update_security = {
	set_variable = { GNG_security_status_var = GNG_security_status_var_temp }
	hidden_effect = {
		remove_ideas = {
			GNG_kenpeitai_pervasive_kenpeitai_networks_dummy
			GNG_kenpeitai_blunt_force_policing_dummy
			GNG_kenpeitai_transitional_security_apparatus_dummy
			GNG_kenpeitai_two_tier_local_policing_dummy
			GNG_kenpeitai_the_guangdong_network_dummy
			GNG_kenpeitai_the_panopticon_dummy
			GNG_kenpeitai_the_militarized_state_dummy
			GNG_kenpeitai_the_IJA_state_dummy
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					GNG_security_status_var = 7
				}
			}
			add_ideas = GNG_kenpeitai_the_IJA_state_dummy
			set_variable = { GNG_security_non_japanese_support_cap = -80 }
			set_variable = { GNG_security_republic_of_china_support_cap = -100 }
			set_variable = { GNG_security_kenpeitai_support_cap = 0 }
			set_variable = { GNG_security_police_support_cap = -90 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					GNG_security_status_var = 6
				}
			}
			add_ideas = GNG_kenpeitai_the_militarized_state_dummy
			set_variable = { GNG_security_non_japanese_support_cap = -40 }
			set_variable = { GNG_security_republic_of_china_support_cap = -50 }
			set_variable = { GNG_security_kenpeitai_support_cap = -0 }
			set_variable = { GNG_security_police_support_cap = -70 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					GNG_security_status_var = 5
				}
			}
			add_ideas = GNG_kenpeitai_blunt_force_policing_dummy
			set_variable = { GNG_security_non_japanese_support_cap = -30 }
			set_variable = { GNG_security_republic_of_china_support_cap = -40 }
			set_variable = { GNG_security_kenpeitai_support_cap = 0 }
			set_variable = { GNG_security_police_support_cap = -65 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					GNG_security_status_var = 4
				}
			}
			add_ideas = GNG_kenpeitai_transitional_security_apparatus_dummy
			set_variable = { GNG_security_non_japanese_support_cap = -15 }
			set_variable = { GNG_security_republic_of_china_support_cap = -15 }
			set_variable = { GNG_security_kenpeitai_support_cap = 0 }
			set_variable = { GNG_security_police_support_cap = -45 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					GNG_security_status_var = 3
				}
			}
			add_ideas = GNG_kenpeitai_two_tier_local_policing_dummy
			set_variable = { GNG_security_non_japanese_support_cap = -5 }
			set_variable = { GNG_security_republic_of_china_support_cap = -5 }
			set_variable = { GNG_security_kenpeitai_support_cap = -65 }
			set_variable = { GNG_security_police_support_cap = 0 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					GNG_security_status_var = 2
				}
			}
			add_ideas = GNG_kenpeitai_the_guangdong_network_dummy
			set_variable = { GNG_security_non_japanese_support_cap = -10 }
			set_variable = { GNG_security_republic_of_china_support_cap = -20 }
			set_variable = { GNG_security_kenpeitai_support_cap = -60 }
			set_variable = { GNG_security_police_support_cap = 0 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					GNG_security_status_var = 1
				}
			}
			add_ideas = GNG_kenpeitai_the_panopticon_dummy
			set_variable = { GNG_security_non_japanese_support_cap = -25 }
			set_variable = { GNG_security_republic_of_china_support_cap = -35 }
			set_variable = { GNG_security_kenpeitai_support_cap = -65 }
			set_variable = { GNG_security_police_support_cap = 0 }
		}
		else = {
			add_ideas = GNG_kenpeitai_pervasive_kenpeitai_networks_dummy
			set_variable = { GNG_security_non_japanese_support_cap = -20 }
			set_variable = { GNG_security_republic_of_china_support_cap = -25 }
			set_variable = { GNG_security_kenpeitai_support_cap = 0 }
			set_variable = { GNG_security_police_support_cap = -55 }
		}
	}
	force_update_dynamic_modifier = yes
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = {
				check_variable = { GNG_security_status_var_temp = 7 }
			}
		}
		GNG_update_underworld_display = yes
	}
	add_to_variable = { GNG_map_dirty_variable = 0.01 }
	add_to_variable = { GNG_product_decisions_dirty_variable = 0.01 }
	add_to_variable = { GNG_3E_dirty_variable = 0.01 }
	add_to_variable = { GNG_economy_dirty_variable = 0.01 }
	custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_update_security_status_tt
}

GNG_corruption_calc = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_corruption_var < 20.01 }
		}
		set_variable = { GNG_corruption_pp_impact = 0.15 }
		set_variable = { GNG_corruption_rGDP_impact = 0.25 }
		set_variable = { GNG_corruption_Government_Support_impact = 0.125 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_corruption_var > 20 }
			check_variable = { GNG_corruption_var < 40.01 }
		}
		set_variable = { GNG_corruption_pp_impact = 0.05 }
		set_variable = { GNG_corruption_rGDP_impact = 0 }
		set_variable = { GNG_corruption_Government_Support_impact = 0.05 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_corruption_var > 40 }
			check_variable = { GNG_corruption_var < 60.01 }
		}
		set_variable = { GNG_corruption_pp_impact = 0.0 }
		set_variable = { GNG_corruption_rGDP_impact = -0.25 }
		set_variable = { GNG_corruption_Government_Support_impact = 0.0 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_corruption_var > 60 }
			check_variable = { GNG_corruption_var < 80.01 }
		}
		set_variable = { GNG_corruption_pp_impact = -0.05 }
		set_variable = { GNG_corruption_rGDP_impact = -0.5 }
		set_variable = { GNG_corruption_Government_Support_impact = -0.05 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_corruption_var < 100.01 }
		}
		set_variable = { GNG_corruption_pp_impact = -0.15 }
		set_variable = { GNG_corruption_rGDP_impact = -0.3 }
		set_variable = { GNG_corruption_Government_Support_impact = -0.10 }
	}
	GNG_calculate_rGDP = yes
}

GNG_corruption_tick = {
	add_to_variable = { GNG_corruption_var = modifier@GNG_monthly_corruption }
	GNG_clamp_three_evils = yes
}

############################
###    Costs and Revenue ###
############################

GNG_misc_income_change = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { #Subtracts from misc costs instead of adding to misc income
				check_variable = { GNG_status_misc_costs_modifier = 0 }
			}
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { GNG_status_misc_costs_modifier = GNG_misc_income_temp }
	}
	else = {
		add_to_variable = { GNG_status_misc_income_modifier = GNG_misc_income_temp }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_misc_income_temp < 0 }
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = {
			var = GNG_misc_income_temp
			value = -1
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_misc_income_decrease_tt
	}
	else = {
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_misc_income_increase_tt
	}
	GNG_calc_misc_econ = yes
	update_economy_tab = yes
}

GNG_misc_costs_change = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { #Subtracts from misc income instead of adding to misc costs
				check_variable = { GNG_status_misc_income_modifier = 0 }
			}
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { GNG_status_misc_income_modifier = GNG_misc_costs_temp }
	}
	else = {
		add_to_variable = { GNG_status_misc_costs_modifier = GNG_misc_costs_temp }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_misc_costs_temp < 0 }
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = {
			var = GNG_misc_costs_temp
			value = -1
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_misc_costs_decrease_tt
	}
	else = {
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_misc_costs_increase_tt
	}
	GNG_calc_misc_econ = yes
	update_economy_tab = yes
}

GNG_calc_misc_econ = { #Checks that you never have negative costs or income
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_status_misc_costs_modifier < 0 }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { GNG_status_misc_income_modifier = GNG_status_misc_costs_modifier  }
		set_variable = { GNG_status_misc_costs_modifier = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_status_misc_income_modifier < 0 }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { GNG_status_misc_costs_modifier = GNG_status_misc_income_modifier  }
		set_variable = { GNG_status_misc_income_modifier = 0 }
	}
}

GNG_setup_demographics = {
	clear_array = GNG_urban_states
	clear_array = GNG_rural_states
	add_to_array = { GNG_rural_states = 593 }
	add_to_array = { GNG_rural_states = 1439 }
	add_to_array = { GNG_rural_states = 1438 }
	add_to_array = { GNG_rural_states = 1017 }
	add_to_array = { GNG_urban_states = 592 }
	add_to_array = { GNG_urban_states = 729 }
	add_to_array = { GNG_urban_states = 326 }

	592 = { #Guangzhou
		set_variable = { jap_pop = 30 }
		set_variable = { zhu_pop = 24 }
		set_variable = { chi_pop = 46 }

		set_variable = { jap_app = 82 }
		set_variable = { zhu_app = 58 }
		set_variable = { chi_app = 56 }
	}
	729 = { #Macao
		set_variable = { jap_pop = 33 }
		set_variable = { zhu_pop = 26 }
		set_variable = { chi_pop = 41 }

		set_variable = { jap_app = 76 }
		set_variable = { zhu_app = 61 }
		set_variable = { chi_app = 59 }
	}
	326 = { #Hong Kong
		set_variable = { jap_pop = 29 }
		set_variable = { zhu_pop = 23 }
		set_variable = { chi_pop = 48 }

		set_variable = { jap_app = 77 }
		set_variable = { zhu_app = 65 }
		set_variable = { chi_app = 54 }
	}
	1439 = { #Shaoguan
		set_variable = { jap_pop = 6 }
		set_variable = { zhu_pop = 18 }
		set_variable = { chi_pop = 76 }

		set_variable = { jap_app = 69 }
		set_variable = { zhu_app = 52 }
		set_variable = { chi_app = 46 }
	}
	1438 = { #Zhaoqing
		set_variable = { jap_pop = 8 }

		set_variable = { chi_pop = 71 }

		set_variable = { jap_app = 58 }

	GNG_update_demographic_display = yes

GNG_update_demographic_display = {
	set_temp_variable = { total_pop_jap = 0 }
	set_temp_variable = { total_pop_zhu = 0 }
	set_temp_variable = { total_pop_chi = 0 }

	set_variable = { total_national_jap_pop_percent = 0 }
	set_variable = { total_national_zhu_pop_percent = 0 }
	set_variable = { total_national_chi_pop_percent = 0 }

	set_variable = { GNG_jap_app = 0 }
	set_variable = { GNG_zhu_app = 0 }
	set_variable = { GNG_chi_app = 0 }

	for_each_loop = {
		array = GNG_states_list
		value = state

		# Normalize values to be /100
		clamp_variable = { var = state:jap_pop min = 0 max = 100 }
		clamp_variable = { var = state:zhu_pop min = 0 max = 100 }
		clamp_variable = { var = state:chi_pop min = 0 max = 100 }

		clamp_variable = { var = state:jap_app min = 0 max = 100 }
		clamp_variable = { var = state:zhu_app min = 0 max = 100 }
		clamp_variable = { var = state:chi_app min = 0 max = 100 }

		set_temp_variable = { total_national_jap_pop_calc = state:state_population_k }
		multiply_temp_variable = { total_national_jap_pop_calc = state:jap_pop }
		divide_temp_variable = { total_national_jap_pop_calc = 100 }
		add_to_variable = { total_national_jap_pop_percent = total_national_jap_pop_calc }

		set_temp_variable = { total_national_zhu_pop_calc = state:state_population_k }
		multiply_temp_variable = { total_national_zhu_pop_calc = state:zhu_pop }
		divide_temp_variable = { total_national_zhu_pop_calc = 100 }
		add_to_variable = { total_national_zhu_pop_percent = total_national_zhu_pop_calc }

		set_temp_variable = { total_national_chi_pop_calc = state:state_population_k }
		multiply_temp_variable = { total_national_chi_pop_calc = state:chi_pop }
		divide_temp_variable = { total_national_chi_pop_calc = 100 }
		add_to_variable = { total_national_chi_pop_percent = total_national_chi_pop_calc }

		set_temp_variable = { total = state:jap_pop }
		add_to_temp_variable = { total = state:zhu_pop }
		add_to_temp_variable = { total = state:chi_pop }
		divide_temp_variable = { total = 100 }
		divide_variable = { state:jap_pop = total }
		divide_variable = { state:zhu_pop = total }
		divide_variable = { state:chi_pop = total }

		set_variable = { state:jap_display = state:jap_pop }

		set_variable = { state:zhu_display = state:jap_pop }
		round_variable = state:zhu_display
		multiply_variable = { state:zhu_display = 1000 }
		add_to_variable = { state:zhu_display = state:zhu_pop }
		add_to_variable = { state:zhu_display = state:jap_pop }

		set_variable = { state:chi_display = state:jap_pop }
		add_to_variable = { state:chi_display = state:zhu_pop }
		round_variable = state:chi_display
		multiply_variable = { state:chi_display = 1000 }
		add_to_variable = { state:chi_display = state:chi_pop }
		add_to_variable = { state:chi_display = state:zhu_pop }
		add_to_variable = { state:chi_display = state:jap_pop }


		# Factor in approval into global approval
		set_temp_variable = { jap_pop_w = state:state_population_k }
		multiply_temp_variable = { jap_pop_w = state:jap_pop }
		divide_temp_variable = { jap_pop_w = 1000 }

		set_temp_variable = { zhu_pop_w = state:state_population_k }
		multiply_temp_variable = { zhu_pop_w = state:zhu_pop }
		divide_temp_variable = { zhu_pop_w = 1000 }

		set_temp_variable = { chi_pop_w = state:state_population_k }
		multiply_temp_variable = { chi_pop_w = state:chi_pop }
		divide_temp_variable = { chi_pop_w = 1000 }

		set_temp_variable = { jap_app_weighted = state:jap_app }
		multiply_temp_variable = { jap_app_weighted = jap_pop_w }

		set_temp_variable = { zhu_app_weighted = state:zhu_app }
		multiply_temp_variable = { zhu_app_weighted = zhu_pop_w }

		set_temp_variable = { chi_app_weighted = state:chi_app }
		multiply_temp_variable = { chi_app_weighted = chi_pop_w }

		add_to_temp_variable = { total_pop_jap = jap_pop_w }
		add_to_temp_variable = { total_pop_zhu = zhu_pop_w }
		add_to_temp_variable = { total_pop_chi = chi_pop_w }

		add_to_variable = { GNG_jap_app = jap_app_weighted }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_zhu_app = zhu_app_weighted }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_chi_app = chi_app_weighted }
	}

	log = "[?GNG_jap_app] japan [?GNG_zhu_app] zhujin [?GNG_chi_app] chinese"

	divide_variable = { total_national_jap_pop_percent = max_manpower_k }
	divide_variable = { total_national_zhu_pop_percent = max_manpower_k }
	divide_variable = { total_national_chi_pop_percent = max_manpower_k }

	divide_variable = { GNG_jap_app = total_pop_jap }
	divide_variable = { GNG_zhu_app = total_pop_zhu }
	divide_variable = { GNG_chi_app = total_pop_chi }

	set_variable = { GNG_jap_app_cap = this.modifier@GNG_japanese_support_cap }
	add_to_variable = { GNG_jap_app_cap = 100 }
	set_variable = { GNG_zhu_app_cap = this.modifier@GNG_zhujin_support_cap }
	add_to_variable = { GNG_zhu_app_cap = 100 }
	set_variable = { GNG_chi_app_cap = this.modifier@GNG_chinese_support_cap }
	add_to_variable = { GNG_chi_app_cap = 100 }
	clamp_variable = {
		var = GNG_jap_app_cap
		min = 0
		max = 100
	}
	clamp_variable = {
		var = GNG_zhu_app_cap
		min = 0
		max = 100
	}
	clamp_variable = {
		var = GNG_chi_app_cap
		min = 0
		max = 100
	}

	clamp_variable = {
		var = GNG_jap_app
		min = 0
		max = GNG_jap_app_cap
	}
	clamp_variable = {
		var = GNG_zhu_app
		min = 0
		max = GNG_zhu_app_cap
	}
	clamp_variable = {
		var = GNG_chi_app
		min = 0
		max = GNG_chi_app_cap
	}
	GNG_calc_demographics_effects = yes
	add_to_variable = { GNG_map_dirty_variable = 0.01 }
}

GNG_calc_demographics_effects = {
	set_variable = { GNG_japanese_gov_support_Empire_Of_Japan_cap = GNG_jap_app }
	subtract_from_variable = { GNG_japanese_gov_support_Empire_Of_Japan_cap = 50 }
	divide_variable = { GNG_japanese_gov_support_Empire_Of_Japan_cap = 4 }

	set_variable = { GNG_japanese_gov_support_pp_gain = GNG_jap_app }
	subtract_from_variable = { GNG_japanese_gov_support_pp_gain = 50 }
	divide_variable = { GNG_japanese_gov_support_pp_gain = 250 }

	set_variable = { GNG_japanese_gov_support_gdp_growth = GNG_jap_app }
	subtract_from_variable = { GNG_japanese_gov_support_gdp_growth = 50 }
	multiply_variable = { GNG_japanese_gov_support_gdp_growth = 0.003 }

	set_variable = { GNG_zhujin_gov_support_corruption = GNG_zhu_app }
	subtract_from_variable = { GNG_zhujin_gov_support_corruption = 50 }
	multiply_variable = { GNG_zhujin_gov_support_corruption = 0.015 }
	multiply_variable = { GNG_zhujin_gov_support_corruption = -1 }

	set_variable = { GNG_zhujin_gov_support_rgdp_growth = GNG_zhu_app }
	subtract_from_variable = { GNG_zhujin_gov_support_rgdp_growth = 50 }
	multiply_variable = { GNG_zhujin_gov_support_rgdp_growth = 0.02 }

	set_variable = { GNG_zhujin_gov_support_conversion = GNG_zhu_app }
	subtract_from_variable = { GNG_zhujin_gov_support_conversion = 50 }
	divide_variable = { GNG_zhujin_gov_support_conversion = 250 }

	set_variable = { GNG_zhujin_gov_support_inverse_conversion = GNG_zhujin_gov_support_conversion }
	multiply_variable = { GNG_zhujin_gov_support_inverse_conversion = -1 }

	set_variable = { GNG_chinese_gov_support_rgdp_growth = GNG_chi_app }
	subtract_from_variable = { GNG_chinese_gov_support_rgdp_growth = 50 }
	multiply_variable = { GNG_chinese_gov_support_rgdp_growth = 0.015 }

	set_variable = { GNG_chinese_gov_support_ROC_opinion_cap = GNG_chi_app }
	subtract_from_variable = { GNG_chinese_gov_support_ROC_opinion_cap = 50 }
	divide_variable = { GNG_chinese_gov_support_ROC_opinion_cap = 4 }

	set_variable = { GNG_chinese_gov_support_conversion = GNG_chi_app }
	subtract_from_variable = { GNG_chinese_gov_support_conversion = 65 }
	if = { #Ensures that the Zhujin to Chinese Con½version makes as much sense as possible
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				GNG_chinese_gov_support_conversion > 0
			}
		}
		divide_variable = { GNG_chinese_gov_support_conversion = 500 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			AND = {
				check_variable = {
					GNG_chinese_gov_support_conversion < 0
				}
				check_variable = {
					GNG_chinese_gov_support_conversion > -30.1
				}
			}
		}
		set_variable = { GNG_chinese_gov_support_conversion = 0 }
	}
	else = {
		add_to_variable = { GNG_chinese_gov_support_conversion = 30 }
		divide_variable = { GNG_chinese_gov_support_conversion = 150 }
	}
	set_variable = { GNG_chinese_gov_support_inverse_conversion = GNG_chinese_gov_support_conversion }
	multiply_variable = { GNG_chinese_gov_support_inverse_conversion = -1 }
	force_update_dynamic_modifier = yes
}

GNG_monthly_demographics_pulse = {
	for_each_loop = { #Chinese-Zhujin conversion
		array = GNG_states_list
		value = state
		if = { #From Chinese to Zhujin
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					this.modifier@GNG_chinese_to_zhujin_conversion > 0
				}
			}
			set_temp_variable = { calc_chi_pop_conversion = state:chi_pop }
			multiply_temp_variable = { calc_chi_pop_conversion = this.modifier@GNG_chinese_to_zhujin_conversion }
			divide_temp_variable = { calc_chi_pop_conversion = 100 }
			add_to_variable = { state:zhu_pop = calc_chi_pop_conversion }
			subtract_from_variable = { state:chi_pop = calc_chi_pop_conversion }
		}
		else_if = { #From Zhujin to Chinese
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					this.modifier@GNG_chinese_to_zhujin_conversion < 0
				}
			}
			set_temp_variable = { calc_zhu_pop_conversion = state:zhu_pop }
			multiply_temp_variable = { calc_zhu_pop_conversion = this.modifier@GNG_chinese_to_zhujin_conversion }
			multiply_temp_variable = { calc_zhu_pop_conversion = -1 }
			divide_temp_variable = { calc_zhu_pop_conversion = 100 }
			add_to_variable = { state:chi_pop = calc_zhu_pop_conversion }
			subtract_from_variable = { state:zhu_pop = calc_zhu_pop_conversion }
		}
	}
	for_each_loop = {
		array = GNG_urban_states
		value = state
		clamp_variable = {
			var = state:chi_pop
			min = 25
			max = 60
		}
		clamp_variable = {
			var = state:zhu_pop
			min = 10
			max = 45
		}
	}
	for_each_loop = {
		array = GNG_rural_states
		value = state
		clamp_variable = {
			var = state:chi_pop
			min = 55
			max = 90
		}
		clamp_variable = {
			var = state:zhu_pop
			min = 5
			max = 40
		}
	}
	for_each_loop = { #Government Support Monthly Changes
		array = GNG_states_list
		value = state
		add_to_variable = { state:jap_app = state:GNG_japanese_gov_support_change }
		add_to_variable = { state:zhu_app = state:GNG_zhujin_gov_support_change }
		add_to_variable = { state:chi_app = state:GNG_chinese_gov_support_change }
	}
	GNG_update_demographic_display = yes
}

###     Underworld    ###
#########################

GNG_police_control_change = {
	add_to_variable = { sar_spt = sar_spt_temp }
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { sar_spt_temp < 0 }
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = {
			var = sar_spt_temp
			value = -1
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_sar_spt_temp_decrease_tt
	}
	else = {
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_sar_spt_temp_increase_tt
	}
	GNG = { GNG_update_underworld_display = yes }
}

GNG_police_control_change_specific_state = { #For Tooltip's sake when you pick a specific state instead of random
	add_to_variable = { sar_spt = sar_spt_temp }
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { sar_spt_temp < 0 }
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = {
			var = sar_spt_temp
			value = -1
		}

	}
	else = {
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_sar_spt_temp_increase_specific_state_tt
	}
	GNG = { GNG_update_underworld_display = yes }
}

	add_to_array = { GNG_states_list = 1439 }
	add_to_array = { GNG_states_list = 1438 }
	add_to_array = { GNG_states_list = 1017 }
	add_to_array = { GNG_states_list = 592 }
	add_to_array = { GNG_states_list = 729 }
	add_to_array = { GNG_states_list = 326 }

	# These don't need to add to 100, they'll be normalized automatically

	592 = { #Guangzhou
		set_variable = { sar_spt = 38 }
		set_variable = { tri_spt = 11 }
		set_variable = { yak_spt = 19 }
		set_variable = { ken_spt = 32 }
	}
	729 = { #Macau
		set_variable = { sar_spt = 28 }
		set_variable = { tri_spt = 25 }
		set_variable = { yak_spt = 15 }
		set_variable = { ken_spt = 32 }
	}
	326 = { #Hong Kong
		set_variable = { sar_spt = 31 }
		set_variable = { tri_spt = 18 }
		set_variable = { yak_spt = 22 }
		set_variable = { ken_spt = 29 }
	}
	593 = { #Chaozhou
		set_variable = { sar_spt = 14 }
		set_variable = { tri_spt = 19 }

	1439 = { #Shaoguan

# This was made so I could make a cool gif
GNG_kickoff_display_tick = {
	set_variable = { tick_ctr = 0 }
	GNG_display_tick = yes
	GNG_initialize_legco = yes
}

GNG_display_tick = {
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { tick_ctr < 800 } }

		set_temp_variable = { k = 0 }

		for_each_loop = {
			array = GNG_states_list
			value = state

			set_temp_variable = { prog = tick_ctr }
			add_to_temp_variable = { prog = k }

			set_temp_variable = { n = prog }
			divide_temp_variable = { n = 200 }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { n = 0.5 }
			round_temp_variable = n
			modulo_temp_variable = { n = 4 }

			modulo_temp_variable = { prog = 200 }
			set_temp_variable = { display = prog }

			set_temp_variable = { display2 = 0 }
			set_temp_variable = { display3 = 0 }

			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { display > 100 } }
				set_temp_variable = { display = 200 }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { display = prog }

				set_temp_variable = { display3 = 100 }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { display3 = display }

			}
			else = {
				set_temp_variable = { display2 = 100 }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { display2 = display }
			}

			set_variable = { state:sar_spt = 0 }
			set_variable = { state:tri_spt = 0 }
			set_variable = { state:yak_spt = 0 }
			set_variable = { state:ken_spt = 0 }

			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { n = 0 } }
				set_variable = { state:sar_spt = display }
				set_variable = { state:tri_spt = display2 }
				set_variable = { state:yak_spt = display3 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { n = 1 } }
				set_variable = { state:tri_spt = display }
				set_variable = { state:yak_spt = display2 }
				set_variable = { state:ken_spt = display3 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { n = 2 } }
				set_variable = { state:yak_spt = display }
				set_variable = { state:ken_spt = display2 }
				set_variable = { state:sar_spt = display3 }
			}
			else = {
				set_variable = { state:ken_spt = display }
				set_variable = { state:sar_spt = display2 }
				set_variable = { state:tri_spt = display3 }
			}

			add_to_temp_variable = { k = 114 }


			set_variable = { state:jap_app = tick_ctr }
			modulo_variable = { state:jap_app = 200 }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { state:jap_app > 100 } }
				set_temp_variable = { show = 200 }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { show = state:jap_app }
				set_variable = { state:jap_app = show }
			}

			set_variable = { state:zhu_app = tick_ctr }
			add_to_variable = { state:zhu_app = 66 }
			modulo_variable = { state:zhu_app = 200 }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { state:zhu_app > 100 } }
				set_temp_variable = { show = 200 }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { show = state:zhu_app }
				set_variable = { state:zhu_app = show }
			}

			set_variable = { state:chi_app = tick_ctr }
			add_to_variable = { state:chi_app = 133 }
			modulo_variable = { state:chi_app = 200 }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { state:chi_app > 100 } }
				set_temp_variable = { show = 200 }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { show = state:chi_app }
				set_variable = { state:chi_app = show }
			}

			set_variable = { state:chi_pop = state:jap_app }
			set_variable = { state:zhu_pop = state:chi_app }
			set_variable = { state:jap_pop = state:zhu_app }
		}
		add_to_variable = { tick_ctr = 10 }
	}

	GNG_update_underworld_display = yes
	GNG_update_demographic_display = yes
	add_to_variable = { GNG_map_dirty_variable = 0.01 }
	#
}


GNG_update_underworld_display = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = GNG_riots_underworld_active
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { sar_states = 0 }
		set_temp_variable = { ken_states = 0 }
		set_temp_variable = { tri_states = 0 }
		set_temp_variable = { yak_states = 0 }
		set_variable = { GNG_majority_controller = 0 }
		set_variable = { GNG_underworld_monthly_corruption = 0 }
		set_variable = { GNG_police_max = 100 }
		set_variable = { GNG_kenpeitai_max = 100 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_police_max = this.modifier@GNG_police_support_cap }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_kenpeitai_max = this.modifier@GNG_kenpeitai_support_cap }

		clamp_variable = {
			var = GNG_police_max
			min = 0
			max = 100
		}
		clamp_variable = {
			var = GNG_kenpeitai_max
			min = 0
			max = 100
		}

		clamp_variable = {
			var = kenpeitai_growth_quarterly_var
			min = 0
		}
		clamp_variable = {
			var = yakuza_growth_quarterly_var
			min = 0
		}
		clamp_variable = {
			var = triad_growth_quarterly_var
			min = 0
		}

		for_each_loop = {
			array = GNG_states_list
			value = state

			# Normalize values to be /100. Clamp Kenpeitai and Police as well
			clamp_variable = { var = state:sar_spt min = 0 max = 100 }
			clamp_variable = { var = state:ken_spt min = 0 max = 100 }
			clamp_variable = { var = state:tri_spt min = 0 max = 100 }
			clamp_variable = { var = state:yak_spt min = 0 max = 100 }

			if = {
				limit = { #This is to avoid weirdness when going over the clamps
					check_variable = {
						var = state:sar_spt
						value = GNG_police_max
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { spt_anchor_divider = 100 }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { spt_anchor_divider = GNG_police_max } #makes sure to divide correctly with the remaning numbers
				set_temp_variable = { total = state:tri_spt }
				add_to_temp_variable = { total = state:ken_spt }
				add_to_temp_variable = { total = state:yak_spt }
				divide_temp_variable = { total = spt_anchor_divider }
				divide_variable = { state:tri_spt = total }
				divide_variable = { state:ken_spt = total }
				divide_variable = { state:yak_spt = total }
				if = {
					limit = { #This is to account for edgecases where both these two are real, which should almost be never
						check_variable = {
							var = state:ken_spt
							value = GNG_kenpeitai_max
							compare = greater_than_or_equals
						}
					}
					set_temp_variable = { ken_spt_anchor = GNG_kenpeitai_max }
					set_variable = { state:ken_spt = ken_spt_anchor }
					set_temp_variable = { ken_anchor_divider = 100 }
					subtract_from_temp_variable = { ken_anchor_divider = GNG_police_max } #makes sure to divide correctly with the remaning numbers
					subtract_from_temp_variable = { ken_anchor_divider = GNG_kenpeitai_max } #makes sure to divide correctly with the remaning numbers
					set_temp_variable = { total = state:tri_spt }
					add_to_temp_variable = { total = state:yak_spt }
					divide_temp_variable = { total = ken_anchor_divider }
					divide_variable = { state:tri_spt = total }
					divide_variable = { state:yak_spt = total }
				}
				set_variable = { state:sar_spt = GNG_police_max }
			}

			else_if = {
				limit = { #This is to avoid weirdness when going over the clamps
					check_variable = {
						var = state:ken_spt
						value = GNG_kenpeitai_max
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
				set_variable = { state:ken_spt = ken_spt_anchor }
				set_temp_variable = { ken_anchor_divider = 100 }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { ken_anchor_divider = GNG_kenpeitai_max } #makes sure to divide correctly with the remaning numbers
				set_temp_variable = { total = state:tri_spt }
				add_to_temp_variable = { total = state:sar_spt }
				add_to_temp_variable = { total = state:yak_spt }
				divide_temp_variable = { total = ken_anchor_divider }
				divide_variable = { state:tri_spt = total }
				divide_variable = { state:sar_spt = total }
				divide_variable = { state:yak_spt = total }
				set_variable = { state:ken_spt = GNG_kenpeitai_max }
			}

			else = { #FIXME Calculations here mean that when you add something the entire value does not get added
				set_temp_variable = { total = state:sar_spt }
				add_to_temp_variable = { total = state:tri_spt }
				add_to_temp_variable = { total = state:ken_spt }
				add_to_temp_variable = { total = state:yak_spt }
				divide_temp_variable = { total = 100 }
				divide_variable = { state:sar_spt = total }
				divide_variable = { state:tri_spt = total }
				divide_variable = { state:ken_spt = total }
				divide_variable = { state:yak_spt = total }
			}
			# Find the controlling faction and by how much they control

			set_variable = { state:controlling_faction = -1 }
			set_temp_variable = { highest_support = 0 }
			set_temp_variable = { second_highest_support = 0 }

			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { state:sar_spt > highest_support } }
				set_variable = { state:controlling_faction = 4 }
				set_temp_variable = { second_highest_support = highest_support }
				set_temp_variable = { highest_support = state:sar_spt }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { state:sar_spt > second_highest_support } }
				set_temp_variable = { second_highest_support = state:sar_spt }
			}

			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { state:tri_spt > highest_support } }
				set_variable = { state:controlling_faction = 1 }
				set_temp_variable = { second_highest_support = highest_support }
				set_temp_variable = { highest_support = state:tri_spt }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { state:tri_spt > second_highest_support } }
				set_temp_variable = { second_highest_support = state:tri_spt }
			}

			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { state:yak_spt > highest_support } }
				set_variable = { state:controlling_faction = 3 }
				set_temp_variable = { second_highest_support = highest_support }
				set_temp_variable = { highest_support = state:yak_spt }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { state:yak_spt > second_highest_support } }
				set_temp_variable = { second_highest_support = state:yak_spt }
			}

			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { state:ken_spt > highest_support } }
				set_variable = { state:controlling_faction = 2 }
				set_temp_variable = { second_highest_support = highest_support }
				set_temp_variable = { highest_support = state:ken_spt }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { state:ken_spt > second_highest_support } }
				set_temp_variable = { second_highest_support = state:ken_spt }
			}

			# Compute # of states from each faction
			# Compute Effects from who owns states

			set_variable = { state:controller_strength = highest_support }
			subtract_from_variable = { state:controller_strength = second_highest_support }

			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { state:controlling_faction = 4 } }
				add_to_temp_variable = { sar_states = 1 }
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { state:controller_strength > 20 }
					}
					add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_monthly_corruption = -0.15 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { state:controller_strength > 10 }
					}
					add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_monthly_corruption = -0.1 }
				}
				else = {
					add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_monthly_corruption = -0.05 }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { state:controlling_faction = 1 } }
				add_to_temp_variable = { tri_states = 1 }
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = GNG_triads_corruption_cancelled
					}
					add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_monthly_corruption = 0.00 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { state:controller_strength > 20 }
					}
					add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_monthly_corruption = 0.075 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { state:controller_strength > 10 }
					}
					add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_monthly_corruption = 0.05 }
				}
				else = {
					add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_monthly_corruption = 0.025 }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { state:controlling_faction = 3 } }
				add_to_temp_variable = { yak_states = 1 }
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = GNG_yakuza_corruption_cancelled
					}
					add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_monthly_corruption = 0.00 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { state:controller_strength > 20 }
					}
					add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_monthly_corruption = 0.15 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { state:controller_strength > 10 }
					}
					add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_monthly_corruption = 0.10 }
				}
				else = {
					add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_monthly_corruption = 0.05 }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { state:controlling_faction = 2 } }
				add_to_temp_variable = { ken_states = 1 }
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = GNG_kenpeitai_corruption_cancelled
					}
					add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_monthly_corruption = 0.00 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { state:controller_strength > 20 }
					}
					add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_monthly_corruption = 0.20 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { state:controller_strength > 10 }
					}
					add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_monthly_corruption = 0.15 }
				}
				else = {
					add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_monthly_corruption = 0.10 }
				}
			}

			# Set up GUI frame
			set_variable = { state:gui_display_frame = state:controlling_faction }
			multiply_variable = { state:gui_display_frame = 1000 }

			set_temp_variable = { control_str_show = state:controller_strength }
			multiply_temp_variable = { control_str_show = 2 }
			clamp_temp_variable = { var = control_str_show min = 0 max = 100 }
			add_to_variable= { state:gui_display_frame = control_str_show }
		}

		#Compute effects based on who is the majority controller
		set_variable = { GNG_triad_control_modifier_china = 0 }
		set_variable = { GNG_triad_control_modifier_japan = 0 }
		set_variable = { GNG_yakuza_control_modifier_gov_support_chinese = 0 }
		set_variable = { GNG_yakuza_control_modifier_gov_support_zhujin = 0 }
		set_variable = { GNG_yakuza_control_modifier_china = 0 }
		set_variable = { GNG_police_control_modifier_gov_support = 0 }
		set_variable = { GNG_police_control_modifier_china_support = 0 }
		set_variable = { GNG_kenpeitai_control_modifier_chinese_government_support = 0 }
		set_variable = { GNG_triad_control_modifier_zhujin_government_support = 0 }
		set_variable = { GNG_triad_control_modifier_china = 0 }

		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { sar_states > 3 } }
			set_variable = { GNG_majority_controller = 4 }
			set_variable = { GNG_police_control_modifier_gov_support = 0.125 }
			set_variable = { GNG_police_control_modifier_china_support = 7.5 }
			set_variable = { GNG_police_control_modifier_japan_support = 5 }
			set_variable = { GNG_police_control_modifier_conversion = 0.1 }
			set_variable = { GNG_police_control_modifier_inverse_conversion = -0.1 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { tri_states > 3 } }
			set_variable = { GNG_majority_controller = 1 }
			set_variable = { GNG_triad_control_modifier_china_support = 5 }
			set_variable = { GNG_triad_control_modifier_japan_support = -7.5 }
			set_variable = { GNG_triad_control_modifier_japanese_government_support = -0.1 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { yak_states > 3 } }
			set_variable = { GNG_majority_controller = 3 }
			set_variable = { GNG_yakuza_control_modifier_gov_support_chinese = -0.075 }
			set_variable = { GNG_yakuza_control_modifier_gov_support_zhujin = -0.05 }
			set_variable = { GNG_yakuza_control_modifier_china = -7.5 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { ken_states > 3 } }
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GNG_kenpeitai_corruption_cancelled
				}
				set_variable = { GNG_majority_controller = 2 }
				set_variable = { GNG_kenpeitai_control_modifier_chinese_government_support = -0.100 }
				set_variable = { GNG_kenpeitai_control_modifier_zhujin_government_support = -0.075 }
				set_variable = { GNG_kenpeitai_control_modifier_china_support = -15 }
			}
			else = {
				set_variable = { GNG_majority_controller = 2 }
				set_variable = { GNG_kenpeitai_control_modifier_chinese_government_support = -0.100 }
				set_variable = { GNG_kenpeitai_control_modifier_zhujin_government_support = -0.075 }
				set_variable = { GNG_kenpeitai_control_modifier_china_support = -15 }
				add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_monthly_corruption = 0.15 }
			}
		}
		force_update_dynamic_modifier = yes
		for_each_loop = {
			array = GNG_states_list
			value = state

			#Calculates monthly government support changes
			set_variable = { state:GNG_japanese_gov_support_change = this.modifier@GNG_monthly_government_support }
			set_variable = { state:GNG_zhujin_gov_support_change = this.modifier@GNG_monthly_government_support }
			set_variable = { state:GNG_chinese_gov_support_change = this.modifier@GNG_monthly_government_support }
			add_to_variable = { state:GNG_japanese_gov_support_change = this.modifier@GNG_monthly_japanese_government_support }
			add_to_variable = { state:GNG_zhujin_gov_support_change = this.modifier@GNG_monthly_zhujin_government_support }
			add_to_variable = { state:GNG_chinese_gov_support_change = this.modifier@GNG_monthly_chinese_government_support }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						state:controlling_faction = 1 #State is controlled by Triads
					}
				}
				if = { #Strong Control
					limit = {
						check_variable = { state:controller_strength > 20 }
					}
					add_to_variable = { state:GNG_chinese_gov_support_change = 0.20 }
				}
				else_if = { #Middling Control
					limit = {
						check_variable = { state:controller_strength > 10 }
					}
					add_to_variable = { state:GNG_chinese_gov_support_change = 0.125 }
				}
				else = { #Weak Control
					add_to_variable = { state:GNG_chinese_gov_support_change = 0.05 }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						state:controlling_faction = 2 #State is controlled by Kenpeitai
					}
				}
				if = { #Strong Control
					limit = {
						check_variable = { state:controller_strength > 20 }
					}
					add_to_variable = { state:GNG_chinese_gov_support_change = 0.075 }
					add_to_variable = { state:GNG_zhujin_gov_support_change = 0.075 }
					add_to_variable = { state:GNG_japanese_gov_support_change = 0.075 }
				}
				else_if = { #Middling Control
					limit = {
						check_variable = { state:controller_strength > 10 }
					}
					add_to_variable = { state:GNG_chinese_gov_support_change = 0.05 }
					add_to_variable = { state:GNG_zhujin_gov_support_change = 0.05 }
					add_to_variable = { state:GNG_japanese_gov_support_change = 0.05 }
				}
				else = { #Weak Control
					add_to_variable = { state:GNG_chinese_gov_support_change = 0.025 }
					add_to_variable = { state:GNG_zhujin_gov_support_change = 0.025 }
					add_to_variable = { state:GNG_japanese_gov_support_change = 0.025 }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						state:controlling_faction = 3 #State is controlled by Yakuza
					}
				}
				if = { #Strong Control
					limit = {
						check_variable = { state:controller_strength > 20 }
					}
					add_to_variable = { state:GNG_japanese_gov_support_change = 0.20 }
				}
				else_if = { #Middling Control
					limit = {
						check_variable = { state:controller_strength > 10 }
					}
					add_to_variable = { state:GNG_japanese_gov_support_change = 0.125 }
				}
				else = { #Weak Control
					add_to_variable = { state:GNG_japanese_gov_support_change = 0.05 }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						state:controlling_faction = 4 #State is controlled by Police
					}
				}
				if = { #Strong Control
					limit = {
						check_variable = { state:controller_strength > 20 }
					}
					add_to_variable = { state:GNG_zhujin_gov_support_change = 0.20 }
				}
				else_if = { #Middling Control
					limit = {
						check_variable = { state:controller_strength > 10 }
					}
					add_to_variable = { state:GNG_zhujin_gov_support_change = 0.125 }
				}
				else = { #Weak Control
					add_to_variable = { state:GNG_zhujin_gov_support_change = 0.05 }
				}
			}
		}
		GNG_clamp_three_evils = yes
		GNG_update_demographic_display = yes
	}
	else = {
		GNG_update_riots_underworld_display = yes
	}
	add_to_variable = { GNG_map_dirty_variable = 0.01 }
}

GNG_initialize_riots_underworld = {
	set_variable = { GNG_map_group_select = 0 }
	GNG_save_underworld_stats = yes
	set_country_flag = GNG_riots_underworld_active
	for_each_loop = {
		array = GNG_states_list
		value = state
		if = {
			limit = {
				GNG = {
					check_variable = {
						GNG_legco_faction_in_power = 3
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						state:controlling_faction = 4
					}
				}
				set_variable = { state:govt_spt = 25 }
				add_to_variable = { state:govt_spt = state:sar_spt }
				set_temp_variable = { govt_spt_addition = state:tri_spt }
				divide_temp_variable = { govt_spt_addition = 2 }
				add_to_variable = { state:govt_spt = govt_spt_addition }
				set_variable = { state:riot_spt = 100 }
				subtract_from_variable = { state:riot_spt = state:govt_spt }
			}
			else = {
				set_variable = { state:riot_spt = 100 }
				subtract_from_variable = { state:riot_spt = state:sar_spt }
				set_variable = { state:govt_spt = state:sar_spt }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				GNG = {
					check_variable = {
						GNG_legco_faction_in_power = 4
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						state:controlling_faction = 4
					}
				}
				set_variable = { state:govt_spt = 25 }
				add_to_variable = { state:govt_spt = state:sar_spt }
				if = {
					limit = {
						GNG = {
							has_country_flag = GNG_matsushita_yakuza_ally
						}
					}
					set_temp_variable = { govt_spt_addition = state:yak_spt }
					divide_temp_variable = { govt_spt_addition = 2 }
					add_to_variable = { state:govt_spt = govt_spt_addition }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						GNG = {
							has_country_flag = GNG_matsushita_triad_ally
						}
					}
					set_temp_variable = { govt_spt_addition = state:tri_spt }
					divide_temp_variable = { govt_spt_addition = 2 }
					add_to_variable = { state:govt_spt = govt_spt_addition }
				}
				else = {
					set_temp_variable = { govt_spt_addition = GNG_legco_matsushita_seats }
					divide_temp_variable = { govt_spt_addition = 2 }
					add_to_variable = { state:govt_spt = govt_spt_addition }
				}
				set_variable = { state:riot_spt = 100 }
				subtract_from_variable = { state:riot_spt = state:govt_spt }
			}
			else = {
				set_variable = { state:riot_spt = 100 }
				subtract_from_variable = { state:riot_spt = state:sar_spt }
				set_variable = { state:govt_spt = state:sar_spt }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				GNG = {
					check_variable = {
						GNG_legco_faction_in_power = 5
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						state:controlling_faction = 4
					}
				}
				set_variable = { state:govt_spt = 25 }
				add_to_variable = { state:govt_spt = state:sar_spt }
				if = {
					limit = {
						GNG = {
							has_country_flag = GNG_matsushita_yakuza_ally
						}
					}
					set_temp_variable = { govt_spt_addition = state:yak_spt }
					divide_temp_variable = { govt_spt_addition = 2 }
					add_to_variable = { state:govt_spt = govt_spt_addition }
				}
				set_variable = { state:riot_spt = 100 }
				subtract_from_variable = { state:riot_spt = state:govt_spt }
			}
			else = {
				set_variable = { state:riot_spt = 100 }
				subtract_from_variable = { state:riot_spt = state:sar_spt }
				set_variable = { state:govt_spt = state:sar_spt }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				GNG = {
					check_variable = {
						GNG_legco_faction_in_power = 7
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						state:controlling_faction = 2
					}
				}
				set_variable = { state:govt_spt = 25 }
				add_to_variable = { state:govt_spt = state:ken_spt }
				set_variable = { state:riot_spt = 100 }
				subtract_from_variable = { state:riot_spt = state:govt_spt }
			}
			else = {
				set_variable = { state:riot_spt = 100 }
				subtract_from_variable = { state:riot_spt = state:ken_spt }
				set_variable = { state:govt_spt = state:ken_spt }
			}
		}
	}
	random_owned_state = {
		limit = {
			GNG_is_pearl_river_delta_state = no
		}
		set_variable = { riot_spt = 80 }
		set_variable = { govt_spt = 20 }
		set_state_flag = GNG_rioter_rural_state
	}
	random_owned_state = {
		limit = {
			GNG_is_pearl_river_delta_state = no
			NOT = {
				has_state_flag = GNG_rioter_rural_state
			}
		}
		set_variable = { riot_spt = 80 }
		set_variable = { govt_spt = 20 }
		set_state_flag = GNG_rioter_rural_state
	}
	random_owned_state = {
		limit = {
			GNG_is_pearl_river_delta_state = no
			NOT = {
				has_state_flag = GNG_rioter_rural_state
			}
		}
		set_variable = { riot_spt = 80 }
		set_variable = { govt_spt = 20 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				GNG_legco_faction_in_power = 7
			}
		}
		random_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 326
					state = 729
				}
			}
			set_variable = { riot_spt = 80 }
			set_variable = { govt_spt = 20 }
		}
	}
	remove_mission = GNG_Growing_Kenpeitai_Influence
	remove_mission = GNG_Growing_Yakuza_Influence
	remove_mission = GNG_Growing_Triad_Influence
	remove_mission = GNG_Growing_Police_Influence
	GNG_update_underworld_display = yes
	add_to_variable = { GNG_map_dirty_variable = 0.01 }
}

GNG_save_underworld_stats = {
	#Clears the effects
	for_each_loop = {
		array = GNG_states_list
		value = state
		set_variable = { state:sar_spt_holding_value = state:sar_spt }
		set_variable = { state:tri_spt_holding_value = state:tri_spt }
		set_variable = { state:yak_spt_holding_value = state:yak_spt }
		set_variable = { state:ken_spt_holding_value = state:ken_spt }
	}
	set_variable = { GNG_yakuza_control_modifier_gov_support_chinese = 0 }
	set_variable = { GNG_yakuza_control_modifier_gov_support_zhujin = 0 }
	set_variable = { GNG_yakuza_control_modifier_china = 0 }
	set_variable = { GNG_triad_control_modifier_china_support = 0 }
	set_variable = { GNG_triad_control_modifier_japan_support = 0 }
	set_variable = { GNG_triad_control_modifier_japanese_government_support = 0 }
	set_variable = { GNG_police_control_modifier_gov_support = 0 }
	set_variable = { GNG_police_control_modifier_china_support = 0 }
	set_variable = { GNG_police_control_modifier_japan_support = 0 }
	set_variable = { GNG_police_control_modifier_conversion = 0 }
	set_variable = { GNG_police_control_modifier_inverse_conversion = 0 }
	set_variable = { GNG_kenpeitai_control_modifier_chinese_government_support = 0 }
	set_variable = { GNG_kenpeitai_control_modifier_zhujin_government_support = 0 }
	set_variable = { GNG_kenpeitai_control_modifier_china_support = 0 }
	set_variable = { GNG_underworld_monthly_corruption = 0 }
}

GNG_unload_underworld_stats = {
	clr_country_flag = GNG_riots_underworld_active
	for_each_loop = {
		array = GNG_states_list
		value = state
		set_variable = { state:sar_spt = state:sar_spt_holding_value }
		set_variable = { state:tri_spt = state:tri_spt_holding_value }
		set_variable = { state:yak_spt = state:yak_spt_holding_value }
		set_variable = { state:ken_spt = state:ken_spt_holding_value }
	}
	GNG_update_underworld_display = yes
}
GNG_update_riots_underworld_display = {
	set_variable = { GNG_underworld_riot_strength_modifier = 0 }
	set_variable = { GNG_underworld_riot_radicalism_modifier = 0 }
	set_variable = { GNG_underworld_riot_despair_modifier = 0 }
	set_variable = { GNG_underworld_riot_frustration_modifier = 0 }
	set_variable = { GNG_underworld_riot_stability_modifier = 0 }
	set_variable = { GNG_underworld_riot_pp_modifier = 0 }
	set_variable = { GNG_govt_states = 0 }
	set_variable = { GNG_riot_states = 0 }
	for_each_loop = {
		array = GNG_states_list
		value = state

		# Normalize values to be /100.
		clamp_variable = { var = state:govt_spt min = 0 max = 100 }
		clamp_variable = { var = state:riot_spt min = 0 max = 100 }

		set_temp_variable = { total = state:govt_spt }
		add_to_temp_variable = { total = state:riot_spt }
		divide_temp_variable = { total = 100 }
		divide_variable = { state:govt_spt = total }
		divide_variable = { state:riot_spt = total }

		set_variable = { state:controlling_faction = -1 }
		set_temp_variable = { highest_support = 0 }
		set_temp_variable = { second_highest_support = 0 }

		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { state:govt_spt > state:riot_spt } }
			set_variable = { state:controlling_faction = 6 }
			set_temp_variable = { highest_support = state:govt_spt }
			set_temp_variable = { second_highest_support = state:riot_spt }
		}

		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { state:riot_spt > state:govt_spt } }
			set_variable = { state:controlling_faction = 7 }
			set_temp_variable = { highest_support = state:riot_spt }
			set_temp_variable = { second_highest_support = state:govt_spt }
		}

		# Compute # of states from each faction
		# Compute Effects from who owns states

		set_variable = { state:controller_strength = highest_support }
		subtract_from_variable = { state:controller_strength = second_highest_support }
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { state:controlling_faction = 6 } }
			add_to_variable = { GNG_govt_states = 1 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { state:controller_strength > 30 }
				}
				add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_riot_strength_modifier = -0.07 }
				add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_riot_radicalism_modifier = -0.07 }
				add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_riot_despair_modifier = -0.07 }
				add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_riot_frustration_modifier = -0.07 }
				add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_riot_stability_modifier = 0.025 }
				add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_riot_pp_modifier = 0.05 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { state:controller_strength > 20 }
				}
				add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_riot_strength_modifier = -0.05 }
				add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_riot_radicalism_modifier = -0.05 }
				add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_riot_despair_modifier = -0.05 }
				add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_riot_frustration_modifier = -0.05 }
				add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_riot_stability_modifier = 0.02 }
				add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_riot_pp_modifier = 0.04 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { state:controller_strength > 10 }
				}
				add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_riot_strength_modifier = -0.035 }
				add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_riot_radicalism_modifier = -0.035 }
				add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_riot_despair_modifier = -0.035 }
				add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_riot_frustration_modifier = -0.035 }
				add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_riot_stability_modifier = 0.015 }
				add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_riot_pp_modifier = 0.03 }
			}
			else = {
				add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_riot_strength_modifier = -0.025 }
				add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_riot_radicalism_modifier = -0.025 }
				add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_riot_despair_modifier = -0.025 }
				add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_riot_frustration_modifier = -0.025 }
				add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_riot_stability_modifier = 0.01 }
				add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_riot_pp_modifier = 0.02 }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { state:controlling_faction = 7 } }
			add_to_variable = { GNG_riot_states = 1 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { state:controller_strength > 30 }
				}
				add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_riot_strength_modifier = 0.07 }
				add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_riot_radicalism_modifier = 0.07 }
				add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_riot_despair_modifier = 0.07 }
				add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_riot_frustration_modifier = 0.07 }
				add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_riot_stability_modifier = -0.025 }
				add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_riot_pp_modifier = -0.05 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { state:controller_strength > 20 }
				}
				add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_riot_strength_modifier = 0.05 }
				add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_riot_radicalism_modifier = 0.05 }
				add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_riot_despair_modifier = 0.05 }
				add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_riot_frustration_modifier = 0.05 }
				add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_riot_stability_modifier = -0.02 }
				add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_riot_pp_modifier = -0.04 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { state:controller_strength > 10 }
				}
				add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_riot_strength_modifier = 0.035 }
				add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_riot_radicalism_modifier = 0.035 }
				add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_riot_despair_modifier = 0.035 }
				add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_riot_frustration_modifier = 0.035 }
				add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_riot_stability_modifier = -0.015 }
				add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_riot_pp_modifier = -0.03 }
			}
			else = {
				add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_riot_strength_modifier = 0.025 }
				add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_riot_radicalism_modifier = 0.025 }
				add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_riot_despair_modifier = 0.025 }
				add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_riot_frustration_modifier = 0.025 }
				add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_riot_stability_modifier = -0.01 }
				add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_riot_pp_modifier = -0.02 }
			}
		}
		# Set up GUI frame
		set_variable = { state:gui_display_frame = state:controlling_faction }
		multiply_variable = { state:gui_display_frame = 1000 }

		set_temp_variable = { control_str_show = state:controller_strength }
		multiply_temp_variable = { control_str_show = 2 }
		clamp_temp_variable = { var = control_str_show min = 0 max = 100 }
		add_to_variable= { state:gui_display_frame = control_str_show }
	}
	set_variable = { GNG_majority_controller = 0 }
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { GNG_govt_states > 3 } }
		set_variable = { GNG_majority_controller = 6 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_riot_strength_modifier = -0.5 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_riot_radicalism_modifier = -0.25 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_riot_despair_modifier = -0.5 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_riot_frustration_modifier = -0.5 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { GNG_riot_states > 3 } }
		set_variable = { GNG_majority_controller = 7 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_riot_strength_modifier = 0.5 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_riot_radicalism_modifier = 0.25 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_riot_despair_modifier = 0.5 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_underworld_riot_frustration_modifier = 0.5 }
	}
	force_update_dynamic_modifier = yes
	add_to_variable = { GNG_map_dirty_variable = 0.01 }
}

GNG_government_control_change = {
	add_to_variable = { govt_spt = govt_spt_temp }
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { govt_spt_temp < 0 }
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = {
			var = govt_spt_temp
			value = -1
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_govt_spt_temp_decrease_tt
	}
	else = {
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_govt_spt_temp_increase_tt
	}
	GNG = { GNG_update_underworld_display = yes }
}

GNG_government_control_change_specific_state = { #For Tooltip's sake when you pick a specific state instead of random
	add_to_variable = { govt_spt = govt_spt_temp }
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { govt_spt_temp < 0 }
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = {
			var = govt_spt_temp
			value = -1
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_govt_spt_temp_decrease_specific_state_tt
	}
	else = {
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_govt_spt_temp_increase_specific_state_tt
	}
	GNG = { GNG_update_underworld_display = yes }
}
