#########################
###    GDP Mechanic   ###
#########################

GNG_backfill_graphs = {
	clear_array = GNG_gdp_history
	clear_array = GNG_target_gdp_history
	clear_array = GNG_manchukuo_gdp_history
	clear_array = GNG_gdp_growth_history
	clear_array = GNG_target_gdp_growth_history
	clear_array = GNG_manchukuo_gdp_growth_history

	#Backfill GDP History
	set_temp_variable = { monthly_gdp_growth = GDP_growth_real }
	divide_temp_variable = { monthly_gdp_growth = 12 }
	multiply_temp_variable = { monthly_gdp_growth = GDP }

	set_temp_variable = { man_monthly_gdp_growth = MAN.GDP_growth_real }
	divide_temp_variable = { man_monthly_gdp_growth = 12 }
	multiply_temp_variable = { man_monthly_gdp_growth = MAN.GDP }

	set_temp_variable = { curr_GDP = GDP }
	set_temp_variable = { curr_man_GDP = MAN.GDP }
	for_loop_effect = {
		start = 0
		end = 25
		value = i

		add_to_array = { array = GNG_gdp_history value = curr_GDP index = 0 }
		add_to_array = { array = GNG_manchukuo_gdp_history value = curr_man_GDP index = 0 }

		randomize_temp_variable = {
			var = rand_multiplier
			distribution = binomial
			min = 0.013
			max = 0.018
		}
		set_temp_variable = { delta = rand_multiplier }
		multiply_temp_variable = { delta = monthly_gdp_growth }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { curr_GDP = delta }

		randomize_temp_variable = {
			var = rand_multiplier
			distribution = binomial
			min = 0.01
			max = 0.015
		}
		set_temp_variable = { delta = rand_multiplier }
		multiply_temp_variable = { delta = man_monthly_gdp_growth }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { curr_man_GDP = delta }
	}

	#Backfill GDP Growth History
	set_temp_variable = { monthly_gdp_growth = GDP_growth_real }
	set_temp_variable = { man_monthly_gdp_growth = MAN.GDP_growth_real }

	for_loop_effect = {
		start = 0
		end = 25
		value = i

		add_to_array = { array = GNG_gdp_growth_history value = monthly_gdp_growth index = 0 }
		add_to_array = { array = GNG_manchukuo_gdp_growth_history value = man_monthly_gdp_growth index = 0 }

		randomize_temp_variable = {
			var = rand_multiplier
			distribution = binomial
			min = -0.03
			max = 0.04
		}
		set_temp_variable = { delta = rand_multiplier }
		multiply_temp_variable = { delta = monthly_gdp_growth }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { monthly_gdp_growth = delta }

		#subtract_from_temp_variable = { curr_pGDP = delta }
		randomize_temp_variable = {
			var = rand_multiplier
			distribution = binomial
			min = -0.02
			max = 0.03
		}
		set_temp_variable = { delta = rand_multiplier }
		multiply_temp_variable = { delta = man_monthly_gdp_growth }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { man_monthly_gdp_growth = delta }
	}

	#Backfill Target GDP Graphs - purely to prevent 2 errors
	set_variable = { GNG_GDP_Goal = 21.2 } # Starting GDP
	set_variable = { GNG_Growth_Goal = 0.06 } # Pre-1962 Normal Growth
	for_loop_effect = {
		start = 0
		end = 25
		value = i

		add_to_array = { array = GNG_target_gdp_history value = GNG_GDP_Goal index = 0 }
	}
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_Growth_Goal_temp = GNG_Growth_Goal }
	multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_Growth_Goal_temp = 100 }
	for_loop_effect = {
		start = 0
		end = 25
		value = i

		add_to_array = { array = GNG_target_gdp_growth_history value = GNG_Growth_Goal_temp index = 0 }
	}

	#Backfill Debt History
	clear_array = GNG_debt_ratio_history
	clear_array = GNG_debt_target_1_history
	clear_array = GNG_debt_target_2_history
	clear_array = GNG_debt_target_3_history
	clear_array = GNG_debt_target_4_history

	clear_array = GNG_manchukuo_debt_ratio_history

	set_temp_variable = { curr_debt_to_GDP_ratio = debt_to_GDP_ratio }
	set_temp_variable = { curr_man_debt_to_GDP_ratio = MAN.debt_to_GDP_ratio }

	multiply_temp_variable = { curr_debt_to_GDP_ratio = 100 }
	multiply_temp_variable = { curr_man_debt_to_GDP_ratio = 100 }

	for_loop_effect = {
		start = 0
		end = 25
		value = i

		add_to_array = { array = GNG_debt_ratio_history value = curr_debt_to_GDP_ratio index = 0 }
		add_to_array = { array = GNG_manchukuo_debt_ratio_history value = curr_man_debt_to_GDP_ratio index = 0 }

		randomize_temp_variable = {
			var = rand_multiplier
			distribution = binomial
			min = -0.25
			max = -0.2
		}
		set_temp_variable = { delta = rand_multiplier }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { curr_debt_to_GDP_ratio = delta }

		randomize_temp_variable = {
			var = rand_multiplier
			distribution = binomial
			min = -0.15
			max = -0.1
		}
		set_temp_variable = { delta = rand_multiplier }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { curr_man_debt_to_GDP_ratio = delta }

		add_to_array = { array = GNG_debt_target_1_history value = 25 index = 0 }
		add_to_array = { array = GNG_debt_target_2_history value = 50 index = 0 }
		add_to_array = { array = GNG_debt_target_3_history value = 75 index = 0 }
		add_to_array = { array = GNG_debt_target_4_history value = 100 index = 0 }
	}

	clear_array = GNG_econ_graph_months
	for_loop_effect = {
		start = 0
		end = 25
		value = i

		add_to_array = { GNG_econ_graph_months = i }
	}
	set_variable = { GNG_econ_graph_month = 25 }

	GNG_draw_graphs = yes
}

GNG_econ_graph_monthly_tick = {
	remove_from_array = { array = GNG_econ_graph_months index = 0 }
	remove_from_array = { array = GNG_gdp_history index = 0 }
	remove_from_array = { array = GNG_target_gdp_history index = 0 }
	remove_from_array = { array = GNG_manchukuo_gdp_history index = 0 }
	remove_from_array = { array = GNG_gdp_growth_history index = 0 }
	remove_from_array = { array = GNG_target_gdp_growth_history index = 0 }
	remove_from_array = { array = GNG_manchukuo_gdp_growth_history index = 0 }
	remove_from_array = { array = GNG_debt_ratio_history index = 0 }
	remove_from_array = { array = GNG_debt_target_1_history index = 0 }
	remove_from_array = { array = GNG_debt_target_2_history index = 0 }
	remove_from_array = { array = GNG_debt_target_3_history index = 0 }
	remove_from_array = { array = GNG_debt_target_4_history index = 0 }
	remove_from_array = { array = GNG_manchukuo_debt_ratio_history index = 0 }

	add_to_array = { GNG_econ_graph_months = GNG_econ_graph_month }

	add_to_array = { GNG_gdp_history = GDP }
	add_to_array = { GNG_target_gdp_history = GNG_GDP_Goal }
	add_to_array = { GNG_manchukuo_gdp_history = MAN.GDP }

	add_to_array = { GNG_gdp_growth_history = GDP_growth_real }
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_Growth_Goal_temp = GNG_Growth_Goal }
	multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_Growth_Goal_temp = 100 }
	add_to_array = { GNG_target_gdp_growth_history = GNG_Growth_Goal_temp }
	add_to_array = { GNG_manchukuo_gdp_growth_history = MAN.GDP_growth_real }

	set_temp_variable = { GNG_debt_ratio_temp = debt_to_GDP_ratio }
	multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_debt_ratio_temp = 100 }
	add_to_array = { GNG_debt_ratio_history = GNG_debt_ratio_temp }
	add_to_array = { GNG_debt_target_1_history = 25 }
	add_to_array = { GNG_debt_target_2_history = 50 }
	add_to_array = { GNG_debt_target_3_history = 75 }
	add_to_array = { GNG_debt_target_4_history = 100 }
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_man_debt_ratio_temp = MAN.debt_to_GDP_ratio }
	multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_man_debt_ratio_temp = 100 }
	add_to_array = { GNG_manchukuo_debt_ratio_history = GNG_man_debt_ratio_temp }

	add_to_variable = { GNG_econ_graph_month = 1 }
	GNG_draw_graphs = yes
	hidden_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = GNG_silicon_years_active
				check_variable = { GNG.GDP > MAN.GDP }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_in_power = 3 } #Sony
				}
				country_event = {
					id = guangdong_manchukuointeractions.18
					days = 7
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_in_power = 4 } #Matsushita
				}
				country_event = {
					id = guangdong_manchukuointeractions.19
					days = 7
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_in_power = 5 } #Fujitsu
				}
				country_event = {
					id = guangdong_manchukuointeractions.20
					days = 7
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_in_power = 7 } #Hitachi
				}
				country_event = {
					id = guangdong_manchukuointeractions.21
					days = 7
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

GNG_update_graph_econ_goal = {
	for_loop_effect = {
		start = 0
		end = 25
		value = i

		set_variable = { GNG_target_gdp_history^i = GNG_GDP_Goal }
	}
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_Growth_Goal_temp = GNG_Growth_Goal }
	multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_Growth_Goal_temp = 100 }
	for_loop_effect = {
		start = 0
		end = 25
		value = i

		set_variable = { GNG_target_gdp_growth_history^i = GNG_Growth_Goal_temp }
	}
	GNG_draw_graphs = yes
}


GNG_find_graph_unit = {

	# Determine rounding factor based on range
	set_temp_variable = { unit = 10000 }
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { range < 3 }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { unit = 0.5 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { range < 6 }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { unit = 1 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { range < 12 }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { unit = 2 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { range < 30 }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { unit = 5 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { range < 60 }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { unit = 10 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { range < 120 }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { unit = 20 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { range < 300 }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { unit = 50 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { range < 600 }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { unit = 100 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { range < 1200 }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { unit = 200 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { range < 3000 }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { unit = 500 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { range < 6000 }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { unit = 1000 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { range < 12000 }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { unit = 2000 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { range < 30000 }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { unit = 5000 }
	}
}


GNG_draw_graphs = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				GNG_graph_shown = 1
			}
		}
		clear_array = GNG_guangdong_segments
		clear_array = GNG_target_segments
		clear_array = GNG_target_segments_2
		clear_array = GNG_target_segments_3
		clear_array = GNG_target_segments_4
		clear_array = GNG_manchukuo_segments

		set_temp_variable = { min = GNG_gdp_history^0 }
		set_temp_variable = { max = GNG_gdp_history^0 }
		for_loop_effect = {
			start = 0
			end = 25
			value = i

			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { GNG_gdp_history^i > max } }
				set_temp_variable = { max = GNG_gdp_history^i }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { GNG_target_gdp_history^i > max } }
				set_temp_variable = { max = GNG_target_gdp_history^i }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { GNG_manchukuo_gdp_history^i > max } }
				set_temp_variable = { max = GNG_manchukuo_gdp_history^i }
			}

			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { GNG_gdp_history^i < min } }
				set_temp_variable = { min = GNG_gdp_history^i }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { GNG_target_gdp_history^i < min } }
				set_temp_variable = { min = GNG_target_gdp_history^i }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { GNG_manchukuo_gdp_history^i < min } }
				set_temp_variable = { min = GNG_manchukuo_gdp_history^i }
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				GNG_graph_shown = 2
			}
		}
		clear_array = GNG_guangdong_segments
		clear_array = GNG_target_segments
		clear_array = GNG_target_segments_2
		clear_array = GNG_target_segments_3
		clear_array = GNG_target_segments_4
		clear_array = GNG_manchukuo_segments

		set_temp_variable = { min = GNG_gdp_growth_history^0 }
		set_temp_variable = { max = GNG_gdp_growth_history^0 }
		for_loop_effect = {
			start = 0
			end = 25
			value = i

			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { GNG_gdp_growth_history^i > max } }
				set_temp_variable = { max = GNG_gdp_growth_history^i }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { GNG_target_gdp_growth_history^i > max } }
				set_temp_variable = { max = GNG_target_gdp_growth_history^i }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { GNG_manchukuo_gdp_growth_history^i > max } }
				set_temp_variable = { max = GNG_manchukuo_gdp_growth_history^i }
			}

			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { GNG_gdp_growth_history^i < min } }
				set_temp_variable = { min = GNG_gdp_growth_history^i }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { GNG_target_gdp_growth_history^i < min } }
				set_temp_variable = { min = GNG_target_gdp_growth_history^i }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { GNG_manchukuo_gdp_growth_history^i < min } }
				set_temp_variable = { min = GNG_manchukuo_gdp_growth_history^i }
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				GNG_graph_shown = 3
			}
		}
		clear_array = GNG_guangdong_segments
		clear_array = GNG_target_segments
		clear_array = GNG_target_segments_2
		clear_array = GNG_target_segments_3
		clear_array = GNG_target_segments_4
		clear_array = GNG_manchukuo_segments

		set_temp_variable = { min = GNG_debt_ratio_history^0 }
		set_temp_variable = { max = GNG_debt_ratio_history^0 }
		for_loop_effect = {
			start = 0
			end = 25
			value = i

			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { GNG_debt_ratio_history^i > max } }
				set_temp_variable = { max = GNG_debt_ratio_history^i }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { GNG_debt_target_1_history^i > max }
					check_variable = {
						GNG_fiscal_status_var = 0
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { max = GNG_debt_target_1_history^i }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { GNG_debt_target_2_history^i > max }
					check_variable = {
						GNG_fiscal_status_var = 1
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { max = GNG_debt_target_2_history^i }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { GNG_debt_target_3_history^i > max }
					check_variable = {
						GNG_fiscal_status_var = 2
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { max = GNG_debt_target_3_history^i }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { GNG_debt_target_4_history^i > max }
					check_variable = {
						GNG_fiscal_status_var = 3
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { max = GNG_debt_target_4_history^i }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { GNG_manchukuo_debt_ratio_history^i > max } }
				set_temp_variable = { max = GNG_manchukuo_debt_ratio_history^i }
			}

			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { GNG_debt_ratio_history^i < min } }
				set_temp_variable = { min = GNG_debt_ratio_history^i }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { GNG_debt_target_1_history^i < min }
					check_variable = {
						GNG_fiscal_status_var = 1
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { min = GNG_debt_target_1_history^i }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { GNG_debt_target_2_history^i < min }
					check_variable = {
						GNG_fiscal_status_var = 2
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { min = GNG_debt_target_2_history^i }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { GNG_debt_target_3_history^i < min }
					check_variable = {
						GNG_fiscal_status_var = 3
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { min = GNG_debt_target_3_history^i }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { GNG_debt_target_4_history^i < min }
					check_variable = {
						GNG_fiscal_status_var = 4
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { min = GNG_debt_target_4_history^i }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { GNG_manchukuo_debt_ratio_history^i < min } }
				set_temp_variable = { min = GNG_manchukuo_debt_ratio_history^i }
			}
		}
	}
	# Find minimum and maximum values visible on graph


	log = "[?min] [?max]"

	set_temp_variable = { range = max }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { range = min }

	GNG_find_graph_unit = yes

	divide_temp_variable = { min = unit }
	divide_temp_variable = { max = unit }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { min = 0.6 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { max = 0.6 }
	round_temp_variable = min
	round_temp_variable = max

	multiply_temp_variable = { min = unit }
	multiply_temp_variable = { max = unit }

	set_temp_variable = { range = max }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { range = min }



	log = "[?min] [?max] [?range]"



	# Generate the y axis ticks for our graph
	divide_temp_variable = { range = 200 }
	set_temp_variable = { m2 = max }
	add_to_temp_variable = { m2 = 0.25 }
	set_temp_variable = { k = min }
	clear_array = GNG_econ_graph_vbars
	clear_array = GNG_econ_graph_vbar_offsets

	set_temp_variable = { half_unit = unit }
	divide_temp_variable = { half_unit = 2 }

	while_loop_effect = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { k < m2 }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { label = k }
		add_to_array = { GNG_econ_graph_vbars = label }

		set_temp_variable = { offset = k }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { offset = min }
		divide_temp_variable = { offset = range }
		multiply_temp_variable = { offset = -1 }
		add_to_array = { GNG_econ_graph_vbar_offsets = offset }

		add_to_temp_variable = { k = unit }

		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { k < m2 } }

			subtract_from_temp_variable = { k = half_unit }

			add_to_array = { GNG_econ_graph_vbars = -1.01 }
			set_temp_variable = { offset = k }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { offset = min }
			divide_temp_variable = { offset = range }
			multiply_temp_variable = { offset = -1 }
			add_to_array = { GNG_econ_graph_vbar_offsets = offset }

			add_to_temp_variable = { k = half_unit }
		}
	}



	# Actually generate the graph line segments
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				GNG_graph_shown = 1
			}
		}
		for_loop_effect = {
			start = 0
			end = 24
			value = i

			set_temp_variable = { j = i }
			add_to_temp_variable = { j = 1 }

			set_temp_variable = { hiA = GNG_gdp_history^j }
			set_temp_variable = { loA = GNG_gdp_history^i }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { hiA = min }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { loA = min }
			divide_temp_variable = { hiA = range }
			divide_temp_variable = { loA = range }

			round_temp_variable = hiA
			round_temp_variable = loA

			set_temp_variable = { endpoints = loA }
			multiply_temp_variable = { endpoints = 1000 }
			add_to_temp_variable = { endpoints = hiA }
			add_to_array = { GNG_guangdong_segments = endpoints }




			set_temp_variable = { hiP = GNG_target_gdp_history^j }
			set_temp_variable = { loP = GNG_target_gdp_history^i }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { hiP = min }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { loP = min }
			divide_temp_variable = { hiP = range }
			divide_temp_variable = { loP = range }

			round_temp_variable = hiP
			round_temp_variable = loP

			set_temp_variable = { endpoints = loP }
			multiply_temp_variable = { endpoints = 1000 }
			add_to_temp_variable = { endpoints = hiP }
			add_to_array = { GNG_target_segments = endpoints }



			set_temp_variable = { hiM = GNG_manchukuo_gdp_history^j }
			set_temp_variable = { loM = GNG_manchukuo_gdp_history^i }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { hiM = min }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { loM = min }
			divide_temp_variable = { hiM = range }
			divide_temp_variable = { loM = range }

			round_temp_variable = hiM
			round_temp_variable = loM

			set_temp_variable = { endpoints =loM }
			multiply_temp_variable = { endpoints = 1000 }
			add_to_temp_variable = { endpoints = hiM }
			add_to_array = { GNG_manchukuo_segments = endpoints }
		}

		set_variable = { GNG_econ_manchukuo_y = hiM }
		multiply_variable = { GNG_econ_manchukuo_y = -1 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_econ_manchukuo_y = 200 }

		set_variable = { GNG_econ_potential_y = hiP }
		multiply_variable = { GNG_econ_potential_y = -1 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_econ_potential_y = 200 }

		set_variable = { GNG_econ_actual_y = hiA }
		multiply_variable = { GNG_econ_actual_y = -1 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_econ_actual_y = 200 }
	}

	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				GNG_graph_shown = 2
			}
		}
		for_loop_effect = {
			start = 0
			end = 24
			value = i

			set_temp_variable = { j = i }
			add_to_temp_variable = { j = 1 }

			set_temp_variable = { hiA = GNG_gdp_growth_history^j }
			set_temp_variable = { loA = GNG_gdp_growth_history^i }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { hiA = min }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { loA = min }
			divide_temp_variable = { hiA = range }
			divide_temp_variable = { loA = range }

			round_temp_variable = hiA
			round_temp_variable = loA

			set_temp_variable = { endpoints = loA }
			multiply_temp_variable = { endpoints = 1000 }
			add_to_temp_variable = { endpoints = hiA }
			add_to_array = { GNG_guangdong_segments = endpoints }




			set_temp_variable = { hiP = GNG_target_gdp_growth_history^j }
			set_temp_variable = { loP = GNG_target_gdp_growth_history^i }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { hiP = min }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { loP = min }
			divide_temp_variable = { hiP = range }
			divide_temp_variable = { loP = range }

			round_temp_variable = hiP
			round_temp_variable = loP

			set_temp_variable = { endpoints = loP }
			multiply_temp_variable = { endpoints = 1000 }
			add_to_temp_variable = { endpoints = hiP }
			add_to_array = { GNG_target_segments = endpoints }



			set_temp_variable = { hiM = GNG_manchukuo_gdp_growth_history^j }
			set_temp_variable = { loM = GNG_manchukuo_gdp_growth_history^i }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { hiM = min }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { loM = min }
			divide_temp_variable = { hiM = range }
			divide_temp_variable = { loM = range }

			round_temp_variable = hiM
			round_temp_variable = loM

			set_temp_variable = { endpoints =loM }
			multiply_temp_variable = { endpoints = 1000 }
			add_to_temp_variable = { endpoints = hiM }
			add_to_array = { GNG_manchukuo_segments = endpoints }
		}

		set_variable = { GNG_econ_manchukuo_y = hiM }
		multiply_variable = { GNG_econ_manchukuo_y = -1 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_econ_manchukuo_y = 200 }

		set_variable = { GNG_econ_potential_y = hiP }
		multiply_variable = { GNG_econ_potential_y = -1 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_econ_potential_y = 200 }

		set_variable = { GNG_econ_actual_y = hiA }
		multiply_variable = { GNG_econ_actual_y = -1 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_econ_actual_y = 200 }
	}

	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				GNG_graph_shown = 3
			}
		}
		for_loop_effect = {
			start = 0
			end = 24
			value = i

			set_temp_variable = { j = i }
			add_to_temp_variable = { j = 1 }

			set_temp_variable = { hiA = GNG_debt_ratio_history^j }
			set_temp_variable = { loA = GNG_debt_ratio_history^i }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { hiA = min }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { loA = min }
			divide_temp_variable = { hiA = range }
			divide_temp_variable = { loA = range }

			round_temp_variable = hiA
			round_temp_variable = loA

			set_temp_variable = { endpoints = loA }
			multiply_temp_variable = { endpoints = 1000 }
			add_to_temp_variable = { endpoints = hiA }
			add_to_array = { GNG_guangdong_segments = endpoints }




			set_temp_variable = { hiP = GNG_debt_target_1_history^j }
			set_temp_variable = { loP = GNG_debt_target_1_history^i }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { hiP = min }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { loP = min }
			divide_temp_variable = { hiP = range }
			divide_temp_variable = { loP = range }

			round_temp_variable = hiP
			round_temp_variable = loP

			set_temp_variable = { endpoints = loP }
			multiply_temp_variable = { endpoints = 1000 }
			add_to_temp_variable = { endpoints = hiP }
			add_to_array = { GNG_target_segments = endpoints }


			set_temp_variable = { hiL = GNG_debt_target_2_history^j }
			set_temp_variable = { loL = GNG_debt_target_2_history^i }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { hiL = min }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { loL = min }
			divide_temp_variable = { hiL = range }
			divide_temp_variable = { loL = range }

			round_temp_variable = hiL
			round_temp_variable = loL

			set_temp_variable = { endpoints = loL }
			multiply_temp_variable = { endpoints = 1000 }
			add_to_temp_variable = { endpoints = hiL }
			add_to_array = { GNG_target_segments_2 = endpoints }

			set_temp_variable = { hiD = GNG_debt_target_3_history^j }
			set_temp_variable = { loD = GNG_debt_target_3_history^i }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { hiD = min }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { loD = min }
			divide_temp_variable = { hiD = range }
			divide_temp_variable = { loD = range }

			round_temp_variable = hiD
			round_temp_variable = loD

			set_temp_variable = { endpoints = loD }
			multiply_temp_variable = { endpoints = 1000 }
			add_to_temp_variable = { endpoints = hiD }
			add_to_array = { GNG_target_segments_3 = endpoints }

			set_temp_variable = { hiT = GNG_debt_target_4_history^j }
			set_temp_variable = { loT = GNG_debt_target_4_history^i }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { hiT = min }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { loT = min }
			divide_temp_variable = { hiT = range }
			divide_temp_variable = { loT = range }

			round_temp_variable = hiT
			round_temp_variable = loT

			set_temp_variable = { endpoints = loT }
			multiply_temp_variable = { endpoints = 1000 }
			add_to_temp_variable = { endpoints = hiT }
			add_to_array = { GNG_target_segments_4 = endpoints }

			set_temp_variable = { hiM = GNG_manchukuo_debt_ratio_history^j }
			set_temp_variable = { loM = GNG_manchukuo_debt_ratio_history^i }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { hiM = min }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { loM = min }
			divide_temp_variable = { hiM = range }
			divide_temp_variable = { loM = range }

			round_temp_variable = hiM
			round_temp_variable = loM

			set_temp_variable = { endpoints =loM }
			multiply_temp_variable = { endpoints = 1000 }
			add_to_temp_variable = { endpoints = hiM }
			add_to_array = { GNG_manchukuo_segments = endpoints }
		}

		set_variable = { GNG_econ_manchukuo_y = hiM }
		multiply_variable = { GNG_econ_manchukuo_y = -1 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_econ_manchukuo_y = 200 }

		set_variable = { GNG_econ_potential_y = hiP }
		multiply_variable = { GNG_econ_potential_y = -1 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_econ_potential_y = 200 }

		set_variable = { GNG_econ_potential_y_2 = hiL }
		multiply_variable = { GNG_econ_potential_y_2 = -1 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_econ_potential_y_2 = 200 }

		set_variable = { GNG_econ_potential_y_3 = hiD }
		multiply_variable = { GNG_econ_potential_y_3 = -1 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_econ_potential_y_3 = 200 }

		set_variable = { GNG_econ_potential_y_4 = hiT }
		multiply_variable = { GNG_econ_potential_y_4 = -1 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_econ_potential_y_4 = 200 }

		set_variable = { GNG_econ_actual_y = hiA }
		multiply_variable = { GNG_econ_actual_y = -1 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_econ_actual_y = 200 }
	}
	add_to_variable = { GNG_economy_dirty_variable = 0.01 }
}


#########################
###   Research Team   ###
#########################


# Mission ID blocks:
## 00-04: Experimental infantry equipment
## 05-09: Experimental tank


GNG_initialize_research_team = { #Sets status array to 30 entires of the value 0
	clear_array = GNG_research_team_mission_status
	resize_array = {
		array = GNG_research_team_mission_status
		value = 0
		size = 30
	}
	clear_array = GNG_research_team_mission_progbar
	resize_array = {
		array = GNG_research_team_mission_progbar
		value = 0
		size = 30
	}

	clear_array = GNG_research_team_active_missions
}

GNG_clear_current_missions = { #Sets any array value that is 1 to a 0
	for_each_loop = {
		array = GNG_research_team_active_missions
		index = i
		value = val

		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { GNG_research_team_mission_status^i = 1 } }
			set_variable = { GNG_research_team_mission_status^i = 0 }
		}
	}
}

GNG_setup_infantry_missions = {

	#This sets all values in STATUS array to 0 if they were 1
	GNG_clear_current_missions = yes

	#This clears GNG_research_team_active_missions array
	clear_array = GNG_research_team_active_missions

	add_to_array = { GNG_research_team_active_missions = 0 }
	add_to_array = { GNG_research_team_active_missions = 1 }
	add_to_array = { GNG_research_team_active_missions = 2 }
	add_to_array = { GNG_research_team_active_missions = 3 }
	add_to_array = { GNG_research_team_active_missions = 4 }

	for_each_loop = {
		array = GNG_research_team_active_missions
		index = i
		value = val

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { i < 5 }
				check_variable = { GNG_research_team_mission_status^i = 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { GNG_research_team_mission_status^i = 1 }
		}
	}
}


GNG_setup_tank_missions = {
	GNG_clear_current_missions = yes

	clear_array = GNG_research_team_active_missions

	add_to_array = { GNG_research_team_active_missions = 5 }
	add_to_array = { GNG_research_team_active_missions = 6 }
	add_to_array = { GNG_research_team_active_missions = 7 }
	add_to_array = { GNG_research_team_active_missions = 8 }
	add_to_array = { GNG_research_team_active_missions = 9 }

	for_each_loop = {
		array = GNG_research_team_mission_status
		index = i
		value = val

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { i > 4 }
				check_variable = { i < 10 }
				check_variable = { GNG_research_team_mission_status^i = 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { GNG_research_team_mission_status^i = 1 }
		}
	}
}

GNG_setup_spart_missions = {
	GNG_clear_current_missions = yes

	clear_array = GNG_research_team_active_missions

	add_to_array = { GNG_research_team_active_missions = 10 }
	add_to_array = { GNG_research_team_active_missions = 11 }
	add_to_array = { GNG_research_team_active_missions = 12 }
	add_to_array = { GNG_research_team_active_missions = 13 }
	add_to_array = { GNG_research_team_active_missions = 14 }

	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { i > 9 }
			check_variable = { i < 15 }
			check_variable = { GNG_research_team_mission_status^i = 0 }
		}
		set_variable = { GNG_research_team_mission_status^i = 1 }
	}
}

GNG_setup_helicopter_missions = {
	GNG_clear_current_missions = yes

	clear_array = GNG_research_team_active_missions

	add_to_array = { GNG_research_team_active_missions = 15 }
	add_to_array = { GNG_research_team_active_missions = 16 }
	add_to_array = { GNG_research_team_active_missions = 17 }
	add_to_array = { GNG_research_team_active_missions = 18 }
	add_to_array = { GNG_research_team_active_missions = 19 }

	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { i > 14 }
			check_variable = { i < 20 }
			check_variable = { GNG_research_team_mission_status^i = 0 }
		}
		set_variable = { GNG_research_team_mission_status^i = 1 }
	}
}

GNG_PTRG_Malaya_END = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = GNG_PTRG_Malaya }
		clr_country_flag = GNG_PTRG_Malaya
		set_temp_variable = { GNG_SHO_Success_Counter = 0 }
		clr_country_flag = GNG_PTRG_deccat_visible
		clr_country_flag = GNG_Fujitsu_Rifle
		clr_country_flag = GNG_Matsushita_Rifle
		clr_country_flag = GNG_Sony_Rifle

		delete_unit_template_and_units = {
			division_template = "Experimental Rifle Division"
			disband = no
		}

		set_temp_variable = { target = SHO }
		TNO_clear_num_volunteers = yes


		for_each_loop = {
			array = GNG_research_team_mission_status
			index = i
			value = val

			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { GNG_research_team_mission_status^i = 2 }
					check_variable = { i < 5 }
				}
				add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_SHO_Success_Counter = 1 }
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = yes
			}
			randomize_temp_variable = {
				var = GNG_SHO_Success_Counter
				distribution = uniform
				min = 2
				max = 5
			}
			round_temp_variable = GNG_SHO_Success_Counter
		}

		set_variable = { GNG_Missions_Success_Variable = GNG_SHO_Success_Counter }
		GNG_clear_current_missions = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_mission = GNG_PTRG_deadline
			# Worst possible outcome
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { GNG_SHO_Success_Counter < 2 } }
				country_event = GNG_PTRG.2
				set_variable = { GNG_PTRG_profit_rgdp = 1.5 }
				set_variable = { GNG_PTRG_profit_gdp = 1.5 }
			}
			# 2nd worst outcome
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { GNG_SHO_Success_Counter = 2 } }
				country_event = GNG_PTRG.3
				set_variable = { GNG_PTRG_profit_rgdp = 2.5 }
				set_variable = { GNG_PTRG_profit_gdp = 2.5 }
			}
			# Middle outcome
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { GNG_SHO_Success_Counter = 3 } }
				country_event = GNG_PTRG.4
				set_variable = { GNG_PTRG_profit_rgdp = 3.5 }
				set_variable = { GNG_PTRG_profit_gdp = 3.5 }
			}
			# 2nd best outcome
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { GNG_SHO_Success_Counter = 4 } }
				country_event = GNG_PTRG.5
				set_variable = { GNG_PTRG_profit_rgdp = 3.5 }
				set_variable = { GNG_PTRG_profit_gdp = 4.5 }
			}
			# Best outcome
			else = {
				country_event = GNG_PTRG.6
				set_variable = { GNG_PTRG_profit_rgdp = 4 }
				set_variable = { GNG_PTRG_profit_gdp = 5 }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { alert_id = token:Alert_GNG_PTRG }
			remove_TNO_alert = yes
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_PTRG_end_result
		clear_array = GNG_research_team_active_missions
	}
}

GNG_PTRG_OC_END = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = GNG_PTRG_OC }

		set_country_flag = GNG_PTRG_OC_Holding

			disband = no
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { ITA = { is_in_faction_with = USA } } }
			set_temp_variable = { target = YEM }
			TNO_clear_num_volunteers = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ITA = {
					is_in_faction_with = JAP
				}
			}
			set_temp_variable = { target = IRQ }
			TNO_clear_num_volunteers = yes
		}
		else = {
			set_temp_variable = { target = SNI }
			TNO_clear_num_volunteers = yes

			TNO_clear_num_volunteers = yes
		}

			TNO_clear_num_volunteers = yes
		}

				ITA = {
					is_in_faction_with = JAP
				}
			}
			set_temp_variable = { target = OMA }
			TNO_clear_num_volunteers = yes
		}
		else = {
			set_temp_variable = { target = OMI }
			TNO_clear_num_volunteers = yes
		}

		TNO_clear_num_volunteers = yes
		for_each_loop = {

GNG_JAP_CHI_Rifle_Add = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_flag = GNG_Fujitsu_Rifle_Global }
		set_technology = { experimental_infantry_equipment_fujitsu_1 = 1 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_global_flag = GNG_Matsushita_Rifle_Global }
		set_technology = { experimental_infantry_equipment_matsushita_1 = 1 }
	}
	else = {
		set_technology = { experimental_infantry_equipment_sony_1 = 1 }
	}
}

			has_dlc = "No Step Back"
		}

						tag = JAP

					}
				}

					special_type_slot_1 = smoke_launchers
					special_type_slot_2 = tank_radio_1
					special_type_slot_3 = experimental_auto_loader
				}
				icon = GFX_GNG_SPART_experimental_sony_medium
				upgrades = {
					tank_nsb_engine_upgrade = 5
					tank_nsb_armor_upgrade = 5
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = GNG_Matsushita_SPART_Global }
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						tag = JAP
						tag = CHI
					}
				}
				set_technology = { NSB_experimental_SPART_modules_matsushita = 1 }
			}
			set_technology = { NSB_experimental_SPART_chassis_1 = 1 }
			create_equipment_variant = {
				name = "Type 32 Artillery - Matsushita Modification"
				type = experimental_SPART_chassis_1
				parent_version = 0
				modules = {
					main_armament_slot = MBT_heavy_artillery_2
					turret_type_slot = MBT_three_man_tank_turret
					suspension_type_slot = experimental_wheel_suspension
					armor_type_slot = tank_welded_armor
					engine_type_slot = tank_gasoline_engine
					special_type_slot_1 = smoke_launchers
					special_type_slot_2 = tank_radio_1
				}
				icon = GFX_GNG_SPART_experimental_matsushita_medium
				upgrades = {
					tank_nsb_engine_upgrade = 5
					tank_nsb_armor_upgrade = 5
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = GNG_Fujitsu_SPART_Global }
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						tag = JAP
						tag = CHI
					}
				}
				set_technology = { NSB_experimental_SPART_modules_fujitsu = 1 }
			}
			set_technology = { NSB_experimental_SPART_chassis_1 = 1 }
			create_equipment_variant = {
				name = "Type 32 Artillery - Fujitsu Modification"
				type = experimental_SPART_chassis_1
				parent_version = 0
				modules = {
					main_armament_slot = experimental_computer_assist_turret
					turret_type_slot = MBT_three_man_tank_turret
					suspension_type_slot = tank_torsion_bar_suspension
					armor_type_slot = tank_welded_armor
					engine_type_slot = tank_gasoline_engine
					special_type_slot_1 = smoke_launchers
					special_type_slot_2 = tank_radio_1
				}
				icon = GFX_GNG_SPART_experimental_fujitsu_medium
				upgrades = {
					tank_nsb_engine_upgrade = 5
					tank_nsb_armor_upgrade = 5
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = GNG_Hitachi_SPART_Global }
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						tag = JAP
						tag = CHI
					}
				}
				set_technology = { NSB_experimental_SPART_modules_hitachi = 1 }
			}
			set_technology = { NSB_experimental_SPART_chassis_1 = 1 }
			create_equipment_variant = {
				name = "Type 32 Artillery - Hitachi Modification"
				type = experimental_SPART_chassis_1
				parent_version = 0
				modules = {
					main_armament_slot = experimental_missile_saturation_turret
					turret_type_slot = MBT_three_man_tank_turret
					suspension_type_slot = tank_torsion_bar_suspension
					armor_type_slot = tank_welded_armor
					engine_type_slot = tank_gasoline_engine

				upgrades = {
					tank_nsb_engine_upgrade = 5
					tank_nsb_armor_upgrade = 5
				}
			}
		}
	}
	else = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = GNG_Sony_SPART_Global }
			set_technology = {
				experimental_SPART_equipment_1 = 1
			}
			create_equipment_variant = {
				name = "Type 32 Artillery - Sony Modification"
				type = experimental_SPART_equipment_1
				icon = GFX_GNG_SPART_experimental_sony_medium
				upgrades = {
					tank_art_upgrade = 1
					tank_engine_upgrade = 1
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = GNG_Matsushita_SPART_Global }
			set_technology = {
				experimental_SPART_equipment_1 = 1
			}
			create_equipment_variant = {
				name = "Type 32 Artillery - Matsushita Modification"
				type = experimental_SPART_equipment_1
				icon = GFX_GNG_SPART_experimental_matsushita_medium

					tank_engine_upgrade = 2
				}

		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = GNG_Fujitsu_SPART_Global }
			set_technology = {
				experimental_SPART_equipment_1 = 1

			set_technology = {
				experimental_SPART_equipment_1 = 1
			}
			create_equipment_variant = {

				type = experimental_SPART_equipment_1
				icon = GFX_GNG_SPART_experimental_hitachi_medium
				upgrades = {
					tank_art_upgrade = 2
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

GNG_JAP_CHI_Helicopter_Add = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_flag = GNG_Sony_Helicopter_Global }
		set_technology = { experimental_helicopter_equipment_sony_1 = 1 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_global_flag = GNG_Matsushita_Helicopter_Global }
		set_technology = { experimental_helicopter_equipment_matsushita_1 = 1 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_global_flag = GNG_Fujitsu_Helicopter_Global }
		set_technology = { experimental_helicopter_equipment_fujitsu_1 = 1 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_global_flag = GNG_Hitachi_Helicopter_Global }
		set_technology = { experimental_helicopter_equipment_hitachi_1 = 1 }
	}
}

GNG_product_cycle_event_initializer = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				GNG_product_cycle_tracker = 1 #Cant be 1 as 1 is for 1962, and 1962 starts by focus. Here for posterity
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				GNG_product_cycle_tracker = 2 #1963
			}
		}
		country_event = GNG_Product_Cycle.3
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				GNG_product_cycle_tracker = 3 #1964
			}
		}
		country_event = GNG_Product_Cycle.3
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				GNG_product_cycle_tracker = 4 #1965
			}
		}
		country_event = GNG_Product_Cycle.3
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				GNG_product_cycle_tracker = 5 #1966
			}
		}
		country_event = GNG_Product_Cycle.3
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				GNG_product_cycle_tracker = 6 #1967
			}
		}
		country_event = GNG_Product_Cycle.3
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				GNG_product_cycle_tracker = 7 #1968
			}
		}
		country_event = GNG_Product_Cycle.3
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				GNG_product_cycle_tracker = 8 #1969
			}
		}
		country_event = GNG_Product_Cycle.3
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				GNG_product_cycle_tracker = 9 #1970
			}
		}
		country_event = GNG_Product_Cycle.3
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				GNG_product_cycle_tracker = 10 #1971
			}
		}
		country_event = GNG_Product_Cycle.3
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				GNG_product_cycle_tracker = 11 #1972
			}
		}
		country_event = GNG_Product_Cycle.3
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				GNG_product_cycle_tracker = 12 #1973
			}
		}
		country_event = GNG_Product_Cycle.3
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				GNG_product_cycle_tracker = 13 #1974
			}
		}
		country_event = GNG_Product_Cycle.3
	}
}

GNG_new_product_cycle_start = {
	set_variable = { GNG_product_cycle_company = GNG_product_cycle_company_temp }
	set_variable = { GNG_product_cycle_active = 1 }
	set_variable = { GNG_product_release_deadline_variable = 100 }

	GNG_calc_product_cycle_initial_vars = yes

	set_variable = { GNG_product_cycle_quality_min_temporary_modifier = 0 }
	set_variable = { GNG_product_cycle_quality_max_temporary_modifier = 0 }
	set_variable = { GNG_product_cycle_interest_min_temporary_modifier = 0 }
	set_variable = { GNG_product_cycle_interest_max_temporary_modifier = 0 }
	set_country_flag = { flag = GNG_product_release_deadline_fast_forward_limiter value = 1 days = 90 }

	hidden_effect = {
		activate_mission = GNG_product_release_deadline
		set_temp_variable = { alert_id = token:Alert_GNG_Product_Cycle }
		add_TNO_alert_unless_exists = yes
	}
	randomize_variable = {
		var = GNG_product_quality
		distribution = uniform
		min = GNG_product_cycle_quality_min
		max = GNG_product_cycle_quality_max
	}
	round_variable = GNG_product_quality
	randomize_variable = {
		var = GNG_product_interest
		distribution = uniform
		min = GNG_product_cycle_interest_min
		max = GNG_product_cycle_interest_max
	}
	round_variable = GNG_product_interest
	custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_start_product_cycle_tooltip
	GNG_product_cycle_var_calc = yes
}

GNG_product_cycle_var_calc = {
	clamp_variable = {
		var = GNG_product_quality
		min = 0
		max = 100
	}
	clamp_variable = {
		var = GNG_product_interest
		min = 0
		max = 100
	}

	#display var for progressbar
	set_variable = { GNG_product_performance = GNG_product_quality }
	add_to_variable = { GNG_product_performance = GNG_product_interest }
	divide_variable = { GNG_product_performance = 2 }

	GNG_calc_product_profitability = yes
	add_to_variable = { GNG_product_decisions_dirty_variable = 0.01 }
}

GNG_calc_product_cycle_initial_vars = {
	clamp_variable = {
		var = GNG_product_cycle_quality_min_base
		min = 0
		max = 100
	}
	clamp_variable = {
		var = GNG_product_cycle_quality_max_base
		min = 0
		max = 100
	}
	clamp_variable = {
		var = GNG_product_cycle_interest_min_base
		min = 0
		max = 100
	}
	clamp_variable = {
		var = GNG_product_cycle_interest_max_base
		min = 0
		max = 100
	}

	set_temp_variable = { GNG_product_cycle_quality_min_show = GNG_product_cycle_quality_min_base }
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_product_cycle_quality_max_show = GNG_product_cycle_quality_max_base }
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_product_cycle_interest_min_show = GNG_product_cycle_interest_min_base }
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_product_cycle_interest_max_show = GNG_product_cycle_interest_max_base }

	add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_product_cycle_quality_min_show = this.modifier@GNG_product_cycle_initial_quality_min_modifier }
	add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_product_cycle_quality_max_show = this.modifier@GNG_product_cycle_initial_quality_max_modifier }
	add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_product_cycle_interest_min_show = this.modifier@GNG_product_cycle_initial_interest_min_modifier }
	add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_product_cycle_interest_max_show = this.modifier@GNG_product_cycle_initial_interest_max_modifier }

	add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_product_cycle_quality_min_show = GNG_product_cycle_quality_min_temporary_modifier }
	add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_product_cycle_quality_max_show = GNG_product_cycle_quality_max_temporary_modifier }
	add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_product_cycle_interest_min_show = GNG_product_cycle_interest_min_temporary_modifier }
	add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_product_cycle_interest_max_show = GNG_product_cycle_interest_max_temporary_modifier }

	set_variable = { GNG_product_cycle_quality_min = GNG_product_cycle_quality_min_show }
	set_variable = { GNG_product_cycle_quality_max = GNG_product_cycle_quality_max_show }
	set_variable = { GNG_product_cycle_interest_min = GNG_product_cycle_interest_min_show }
	set_variable = { GNG_product_cycle_interest_max = GNG_product_cycle_interest_max_show }
}

GNG_calc_product_profitability = {
	set_variable = { GNG_product_profitability = 1 }
	add_to_variable = { GNG_product_profitability = GNG_Market_Product_Profitability^GNG_target_market }
	add_to_variable = { GNG_product_profitability = modifier@GNG_product_profitability_modifier }
	add_to_variable = { GNG_product_profitability = GNG_product_profitability_temp_effect }
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_product_cycle_company = 1 }
		}
		set_variable = { GNG_company_specific_profitability = modifier@GNG_Sony_Product_Profitability }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_product_profitability = GNG_company_specific_profitability }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_product_cycle_company = 2 }
		}
		set_variable = { GNG_company_specific_profitability = modifier@GNG_Matsushita_Product_Profitability }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_product_profitability = GNG_company_specific_profitability }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_product_cycle_company = 3 }
		}
		set_variable = { GNG_company_specific_profitability = modifier@GNG_Fujitsu_Product_Profitability }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_product_profitability = GNG_company_specific_profitability }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_product_cycle_company = 4 }
		}
		set_variable = { GNG_company_specific_profitability = modifier@GNG_Hitachi_Product_Profitability }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_product_profitability = GNG_company_specific_profitability }
	}
}

GNG_product_cycle_end = {
	hidden_effect = {
		remove_mission = GNG_product_release_deadline
		#Calculate Effects for Tooltips Sake
		set_variable = { GNG_product_cycle_calc = GNG_product_quality }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_product_cycle_calc = GNG_product_interest }
		divide_variable = { GNG_product_cycle_calc = 2 }

		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = GNG_100_percent_product }
				check_variable = { GNG_product_cycle_calc = 100 }
			}
			set_country_flag = GNG_100_percent_product
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				GNG = {
					is_ai = yes
				}
			}
			randomize_variable = { #Makes the AI somewhat competitive
				var = GNG_product_cycle_calc
				distribution = uniform
				min = 60
				max = 90
			}
			#Forces it so that a player gets the market events
			if = {
				limit = {
					JAP = {
						is_ai = no
					}
				}
				set_variable = { GNG_target_market = 1 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					CHI = {
						is_ai = no
					}
				}
				set_variable = { GNG_target_market = 2 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					ITA = {
						is_ai = no
					}
					has_country_flag = GNG_Post_Yasuda_Markets
				}
				set_variable = { GNG_target_market = 3 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					IBR = {
						is_ai = no
					}
					has_country_flag = GNG_Post_Yasuda_Markets
				}
				set_variable = { GNG_target_market = 4 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					TUR = {
						is_ai = no
					}
					has_country_flag = GNG_Post_Yasuda_Markets
				}
				set_variable = { GNG_target_market = 5 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					MEX = {
						is_ai = no
					}
					has_country_flag = GNG_Post_Yasuda_Markets
				}
				set_variable = { GNG_target_market = 6 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					BRA = {
						is_ai = no
					}
					has_country_flag = GNG_Post_Yasuda_Markets
				}
				set_variable = { GNG_target_market = 7 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					ARG = {
						is_ai = no
					}
					has_country_flag = GNG_Post_Yasuda_Markets
				}
				set_variable = { GNG_target_market = 8 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					CHL = {
						is_ai = no
					}
					has_country_flag = GNG_Post_Yasuda_Markets
				}
				set_variable = { GNG_target_market = 9 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					USA = {
						is_ai = no
					}
					has_country_flag = GNG_America_Market
				}
				set_variable = { GNG_target_market = 10 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					GER = {
						is_ai = no
					}
					has_country_flag = GNG_Germany_Market
				}
				set_variable = { GNG_target_market = 11 }
			}
		}

		set_variable = { GNG_product_cycle_calc_2 = GNG_product_cycle_calc }
		subtract_from_variable = { GNG_product_cycle_calc_2 = 50 }
		multiply_variable = { GNG_product_cycle_calc_2 = 0.06 } # 3 seats +/-
		round_variable = GNG_product_cycle_calc_2

		set_variable = { GNG_Product_Cycle_rGDP = GNG_product_cycle_calc }
		multiply_variable = { GNG_Product_Cycle_rGDP = 0.025 } #2.5% at 100%
		multiply_variable = { GNG_Product_Cycle_rGDP = GNG_product_profitability }
		set_variable = { GNG_Product_Cycle_GDP_growth = GNG_product_cycle_calc }
		multiply_variable = { GNG_Product_Cycle_GDP_growth = 0.06 } #6% at 100%
		multiply_variable = { GNG_Product_Cycle_GDP_growth = GNG_product_profitability }
		set_variable = { GNG_Product_Cycle_misc_income = GNG_product_cycle_calc }
		divide_variable = { GNG_Product_Cycle_misc_income = 80 } #1.25 Bil at 100%
		multiply_variable = { GNG_Product_Cycle_misc_income = GNG_product_profitability }
		set_country_flag = GNG_show_product_cycle_preface

		GNG_initiailize_product_cycle_end_event = yes
		clr_country_flag = GNG_yearly_product_cycle
		clr_country_flag = GNG_show_market_decisions
		clr_country_flag = GNG_show_advertisement_decisions
		clr_country_flag = GNG_show_quality_assurance_decisions
		clr_country_flag = GNG_product_cycle_pushed_forward
		clr_country_flag = GNG_product_cycle_delayed
		set_temp_variable = { alert_id = token:Alert_GNG_Product_Cycle }
		remove_TNO_alert = yes
	}
	add_to_variable = { GNG_product_decisions_dirty_variable = 0.01 }
}

GNG_show_effects_for_product_cycle = {
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_product_cycle_calc = GNG_product_quality }
	add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_product_cycle_calc = GNG_product_interest }
	divide_temp_variable = { GNG_product_cycle_calc = 2 }
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_product_cycle_calc_2 = GNG_product_cycle_calc }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { GNG_product_cycle_calc_2 = 50 }
	multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_product_cycle_calc_2 = 0.06 } # 3 seats +/-
	round_temp_variable = GNG_product_cycle_calc_2
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_Product_Cycle_rGDP = GNG_product_cycle_calc }
	multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_Product_Cycle_rGDP = 0.025 } #2.5% at 100%
	multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_Product_Cycle_rGDP = GNG_product_profitability }
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_Product_Cycle_GDP_growth = GNG_product_cycle_calc }
	multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_Product_Cycle_GDP_growth = 0.06 } #6% at 100%
	multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_Product_Cycle_GDP_growth = GNG_product_profitability }
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_Product_Cycle_misc_income = GNG_product_cycle_calc }
	divide_temp_variable = { GNG_Product_Cycle_misc_income = 80 } #1.25 Bil at 100%
	multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_Product_Cycle_misc_income = GNG_product_profitability }
	custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_show_effects_for_product_cycle_tt
	effect_tooltip = {
		GNG_give_product_cycle_effects = yes
	}
}

GNG_give_product_cycle_effects = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = GNG_show_product_cycle_preface
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_product_cycle_preface
		clr_country_flag = GNG_show_product_cycle_preface
	}
	#Calc how many seats were gained/lost
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_seat_temp = GNG_product_cycle_calc_2 }
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { GNG_product_cycle_company = 1 } } #Sony
		if = { #Pre-CK
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = GNG_legco_stage_2
				}
			}
			set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_temp = 3 }
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { GNG_legco_seat_temp > 1.99 }
				}
				set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_seat_temp_holding = GNG_legco_seat_temp }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_seat_temp_holding = 1 }
				set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_seat_temp = 1 }
				set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_temp = 6 }
				GNG_change_legco_seats = yes
				set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_seat_temp = GNG_legco_seat_temp_holding }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { GNG_legco_seat_temp < -1.99 }
				}
				set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_seat_temp_holding = GNG_legco_seat_temp }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_seat_temp_holding = -1 }
				set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_seat_temp = -1 }
				set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_temp = 6 }
				GNG_change_legco_seats = yes
				set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_seat_temp = GNG_legco_seat_temp_holding }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_temp = 3 }
		}

	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { GNG_product_cycle_company = 2 } } #Matsushita
		set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_temp = 4 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { GNG_product_cycle_company = 3 } } #Fujitsu
		set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_temp = 5 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { GNG_product_cycle_company = 4 } } #Hitachi
		if = { #Suzuki
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = GNG_legco_stage_2
				}
			}
			set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_temp = 2 }
		}
		else = { #Hitachi
			set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_temp = 7 }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = {
				check_variable = { GNG_legco_seat_temp = 0 }
			}
		}
		GNG_change_legco_seats = yes
	}
	custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_product_cycle_idea
	custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_special_market_preface_tt
	GNG_special_market_effects = yes
	hidden_effect = {
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = GNG_the_product_cycle_dummy
			days = 120
		}
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		GNG_product_cycle_quality_min_base = -5
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		GNG_product_cycle_quality_max_base = -5
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		GNG_product_cycle_interest_min_base = -5
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		GNG_product_cycle_interest_max_base = -5
	}
	GNG_calc_product_cycle_initial_vars = yes
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = GNG_show_product_cycle_preface
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_product_cycle_quality_interest_reduction
	}
	hidden_effect = {
		add_dynamic_modifier = {
			modifier = GNG_product_cycle_modifiers
		}
	}
	hidden_effect = {
		country_event = {
			id = GNG_Product_Cycle.100
			days = 120
		}
	}
	set_variable = { GNG_show_days_to_next_cycle_visible = 1 }
	GNG_add_product_to_history = yes
	set_variable = { GNG_product_profitability_temp_effect = 0 }
	GNG_calculate_rGDP = yes
	update_economy_tab = yes
	set_variable = { GNG_product_cycle_company = 0 }
}

GNG_change_market_profitability = {
	add_to_variable = { GNG_Market_Product_Profitability^GNG_market_temp = GNG_market_profitability_temp }
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_market_profitability_temp < 0 }
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = {
			var = GNG_market_profitability_temp
			value = -1
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_market_profitability_temp_decrease_tt
	}
	else = {
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_market_profitability_temp_increase_tt
	}
}

GNG_select_market = {
	set_variable = { GNG_target_market = GNG_market_temp }
	custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_choose_market_tt
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_market_temp = 1 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_japanese_market_effects
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_market_temp = 2 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_chinese_market_effects
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_market_temp < 10 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_post_yasuda_market_effects
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_market_temp < 12 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_superpower_market_effects
	}
	GNG_product_cycle_var_calc = yes
}

GNG_special_market_effects = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				GNG_target_market = 1 #Japan
			}
		}
		#Calcs Japan Approval Gain
		set_temp_variable = { GNG_product_cycle_japan_approval = GNG_product_cycle_calc }
		divide_temp_variable = { GNG_product_cycle_japan_approval = 20 }
		set_temp_variable = { GNG_approval_temp_var = GNG_product_cycle_japan_approval }
		GNG_Japan_approval_change = yes
		random_owned_state = {
			set_temp_variable = { chi_app_temp = -1.5 }
			GNG_chinese_app_change = yes
		}
		random_owned_state = {
			set_temp_variable = { chi_app_temp = -1.5 }
			GNG_chinese_app_change = yes
		}
		random_owned_state = {
			set_temp_variable = { chi_app_temp = -1.5 }
			GNG_chinese_app_change = yes
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				GNG_target_market = 2 #China
			}
		}
		#Calcs China Opinion Gain
		set_temp_variable = { GNG_product_cycle_china_opinion = GNG_product_cycle_calc }
		multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_product_cycle_china_opinion = 0.075 }
		set_temp_variable = { GNG_opinion_temp_var = GNG_product_cycle_china_opinion }
		GNG_China_opinion_change = yes
		random_owned_state = {
			set_temp_variable = { chi_app_temp = 1.5 }
			GNG_chinese_app_change = yes
		}
		random_owned_state = {
			set_temp_variable = { chi_app_temp = 1.5 }
			GNG_chinese_app_change = yes
		}
		random_owned_state = {
			set_temp_variable = { chi_app_temp = 1.5 }
			GNG_chinese_app_change = yes
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				GNG_target_market = 10 #America
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { GNG_approval_temp_var = -3 }
		GNG_Japan_approval_change = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				GNG_target_market = 11 #Germany
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { GNG_approval_temp_var = -3 }
		GNG_Japan_approval_change = yes
	}
	GNG_market_event_picker = yes
}

GNG_add_product_to_history = {
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { GNG_current_product_id > 0 } }
		set_temp_variable = { GNG_product_success_temp = GNG_product_cycle_calc } #Adds the success to the history
		divide_temp_variable = { GNG_product_success_temp = 20 }
		add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_product_success_temp = 0.5 } #Ensures it rounds up
		round_temp_variable = GNG_product_success_temp
		add_to_array = { array = GNG_product_success value = GNG_product_success_temp index = 0 }

		add_to_array = { array = GNG_product_history value = GNG_current_product_id index = 0 } #Adds it to history
		set_variable = { GNG_current_product_id = 0 }
		set_variable = { GNG_target_market = 0 }
		set_variable = { GNG_product_profitability_market_effect = 0 }
		set_variable = { GNG_product_quality = 0 }
		set_variable = { GNG_product_interest = 0 }
		set_variable = { GNG_product_cycle_active = 0 }
	}
}

GNG_product_cycle_interest_change = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_product_cycle_active = 1 }
		}
		add_to_variable = { GNG_product_interest = GNG_product_interest_temp }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GNG_product_interest_temp < 0 }
			}
			multiply_temp_variable = {
				var = GNG_product_interest_temp
				value = -1
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_product_interest_temp_decrease_tt
		}
		else = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_product_interest_temp_increase_tt
		}
		GNG = { GNG_product_cycle_var_calc = yes }
	}
	else = {
		set_temp_variable = { GNG_product_cycle_interest_min_temporary_modifier_temp = GNG_product_interest_temp }
		set_temp_variable = { GNG_product_cycle_interest_max_temporary_modifier_temp = GNG_product_interest_temp }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_product_cycle_interest_min_temporary_modifier = GNG_product_cycle_interest_min_temporary_modifier_temp }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GNG_product_cycle_interest_min_temporary_modifier_temp < 0 }
			}
			multiply_temp_variable = {
				var = GNG_product_cycle_interest_min_temporary_modifier_temp
				value = -1
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_product_cycle_next_product_interest_min_decrease_tt
		}
		else = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_product_cycle_next_product_interest_min_increase_tt
		}
		add_to_variable = { GNG_product_cycle_interest_max_temporary_modifier = GNG_product_cycle_interest_max_temporary_modifier_temp }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GNG_product_cycle_interest_max_temporary_modifier_temp < 0 }
			}
			multiply_temp_variable = {
				var = GNG_product_cycle_interest_max_temporary_modifier_temp
				value = -1
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_product_cycle_next_product_interest_max_decrease_tt
		}
		else = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_product_cycle_next_product_interest_max_increase_tt
		}
		GNG = { GNG_product_cycle_var_calc = yes }
	}
}

### Research and Development ###

GNG_research_modifiers_base_calc = {
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_research_multiplier = this.modifier@GNG_rnd_modifier }
	add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_research_multiplier = 1 }
	for_each_loop = {
		array = GNG_ARR_research_monthly_real
		index = i
		value = val

		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { i < 6 } }
			set_variable = { GNG_ARR_research_monthly_real^i = GNG_ARR_research_monthly_base^i }
			multiply_variable = { GNG_ARR_research_monthly_real^i = GNG_research_multiplier }
		}
	}

	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_field_of_research = 0 }
		}
		set_variable = { GNG_focus_factor_audio_and_video = 0 }
		set_variable = { GNG_focus_factor_household_electronics = 0 }
		set_variable = { GNG_focus_factor_data_storage = 0 }
		set_variable = { GNG_focus_factor_power_efficiency = 0 }
		set_variable = { GNG_focus_factor_computational_power = 0 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_field_of_research = 1 }
		}
		set_variable = { GNG_focus_factor_audio_and_video = 0.25 }
		set_variable = { GNG_focus_factor_household_electronics = -0.1 }
		set_variable = { GNG_focus_factor_data_storage = -0.1 }
		set_variable = { GNG_focus_factor_power_efficiency = -0.1 }
		set_variable = { GNG_focus_factor_computational_power = -0.1 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_field_of_research = 2 }
		}
		set_variable = { GNG_focus_factor_audio_and_video = -0.1 }
		set_variable = { GNG_focus_factor_household_electronics = 0.25 }
		set_variable = { GNG_focus_factor_data_storage = -0.1 }
		set_variable = { GNG_focus_factor_power_efficiency = -0.1 }
		set_variable = { GNG_focus_factor_computational_power = -0.1 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_field_of_research = 3 }
		}
		set_variable = { GNG_focus_factor_audio_and_video = -0.1 }
		set_variable = { GNG_focus_factor_household_electronics = -0.1 }
		set_variable = { GNG_focus_factor_data_storage = 0.25 }
		set_variable = { GNG_focus_factor_power_efficiency = -0.1 }
		set_variable = { GNG_focus_factor_computational_power = -0.1 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_field_of_research = 4 }
		}
		set_variable = { GNG_focus_factor_audio_and_video = -0.1 }
		set_variable = { GNG_focus_factor_household_electronics = -0.1 }
		set_variable = { GNG_focus_factor_data_storage = -0.1 }
		set_variable = { GNG_focus_factor_computational_power = 0.25 }
		set_variable = { GNG_focus_factor_power_efficiency = -0.1 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_field_of_research = 5 }
		}
		set_variable = { GNG_focus_factor_audio_and_video = -0.1 }
		set_variable = { GNG_focus_factor_household_electronics = -0.1 }
		set_variable = { GNG_focus_factor_data_storage = -0.1 }
		set_variable = { GNG_focus_factor_computational_power = -0.1 }
		set_variable = { GNG_focus_factor_power_efficiency = 0.25 }
	}

	force_update_dynamic_modifier = yes

	set_temp_variable = { GNG_research_monthly_multiplier_1 = this.modifier@GNG_rnd_audio_video_modifier }
	add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_research_monthly_multiplier_1 = this.modifier@GNG_rnd_audio_video_focus_modifier }
	add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_research_monthly_multiplier_1 = 1 }

	set_temp_variable = { GNG_research_monthly_multiplier_2 = this.modifier@GNG_rnd_household_electronics_modifier }
	add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_research_monthly_multiplier_2 = this.modifier@GNG_rnd_household_electronics_focus_modifier }
	add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_research_monthly_multiplier_2 = 1 }

	set_temp_variable = { GNG_research_monthly_multiplier_3 = this.modifier@GNG_rnd_data_storage_modifier }
	add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_research_monthly_multiplier_3 = this.modifier@GNG_rnd_data_storage_focus_modifier }
	add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_research_monthly_multiplier_3 = 1 }

	set_temp_variable = { GNG_research_monthly_multiplier_4 = this.modifier@GNG_rnd_computational_power_modifier }
	add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_research_monthly_multiplier_4 = this.modifier@GNG_rnd_computational_power_focus_modifier }
	add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_research_monthly_multiplier_4 = 1 }

	set_temp_variable = { GNG_research_monthly_multiplier_5 = this.modifier@GNG_rnd_power_efficiency_modifier }
	add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_research_monthly_multiplier_5 = this.modifier@GNG_rnd_power_efficiency_focus_modifier }
	add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_research_monthly_multiplier_5 = 1 }

	multiply_variable = { GNG_ARR_research_monthly_real^1 = GNG_research_monthly_multiplier_1 }
	multiply_variable = { GNG_ARR_research_monthly_real^2 = GNG_research_monthly_multiplier_2 }
	multiply_variable = { GNG_ARR_research_monthly_real^3 = GNG_research_monthly_multiplier_3 }
	multiply_variable = { GNG_ARR_research_monthly_real^4 = GNG_research_monthly_multiplier_4 }
	multiply_variable = { GNG_ARR_research_monthly_real^5 = GNG_research_monthly_multiplier_5 }
	add_to_variable = { GNG_product_decisions_dirty_variable = 0.01 }
}

GNG_research_monthly_calc = {
	for_each_loop = {
		array = GNG_ARR_research_bars
		index = i
		value = val

		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { i < 6 } }
			add_to_variable = { GNG_ARR_research_bars^i = GNG_ARR_research_monthly_real^i }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_ARR_research_bars^1 > 99.9 }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { GNG_ARR_research_bars^1 = 100 }
		multiply_variable = { GNG_ARR_research_monthly_base^1 = 0.9 }
		multiply_variable = { GNG_ARR_research_bars^1 = 0.9 }
		country_event = GNG_RnD.1
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_ARR_research_bars^2 > 99.9 }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { GNG_ARR_research_bars^2 = 100 }
		multiply_variable = { GNG_ARR_research_monthly_base^2 = 0.9 }
		multiply_variable = { GNG_ARR_research_bars^2 = 0.9 }
		country_event = GNG_RnD.2
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_ARR_research_bars^3 > 99.9 }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { GNG_ARR_research_bars^3 = 100 }
		multiply_variable = { GNG_ARR_research_monthly_base^3 = 0.9 }
		multiply_variable = { GNG_ARR_research_bars^3 = 0.9 }
		country_event = GNG_RnD.3
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_ARR_research_bars^4 > 99.9 }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { GNG_ARR_research_bars^4 = 100 }
		multiply_variable = { GNG_ARR_research_monthly_base^4 = 0.9 }
		multiply_variable = { GNG_ARR_research_bars^4 = 0.9 }
		country_event = GNG_RnD.4
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_ARR_research_bars^5 > 99.9 }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { GNG_ARR_research_bars^5 = 100 }
		multiply_variable = { GNG_ARR_research_monthly_base^5 = 0.9 }
		multiply_variable = { GNG_ARR_research_bars^5 = 0.9 }
		country_event = GNG_RnD.5
	}
	for_each_loop = {
		array = GNG_ARR_research_bars
		index = i
		value = val

		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { i < 6 } }
			clamp_variable = {
				var = GNG_ARR_research_bars^i
				min = 0
				max = 100
			}
		}
	}
	add_to_variable = { GNG_product_decisions_dirty_variable = 0.01 }
}

GNG_research_base_monthly_change = {
	add_to_variable = { GNG_ARR_research_monthly_base^GNG_RnD_temp_id = GNG_research_monthly_base_temp }
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_research_monthly_base_temp < 0 }
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = {
			var = GNG_research_monthly_base_temp
			value = -1
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_research_base_decrease_tt
	}
	else = {
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_research_base_increase_tt
	}
	GNG = { GNG_research_modifiers_base_calc = yes }
}

GNG_research_base_monthly_change_all = {
	for_each_loop = {
		array = GNG_ARR_research_monthly_base
		index = i
		value = val

		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { i < 6 } }
			add_to_variable = { GNG_ARR_research_monthly_base^i = GNG_research_monthly_base_temp }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_research_monthly_base_temp < 0 }
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = {
			var = GNG_research_monthly_base_temp
			value = -1
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_research_base_all_decrease_tt
	}
	else = {
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_research_base_all_increase_tt
	}
	GNG = { GNG_research_modifiers_base_calc = yes }
}
