GNG_hit_GDP_target_effect = {
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_seat_temp = 3 }
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_temp = GNG_legco_faction_in_power }
	GNG_change_legco_seats = yes
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_Next_Year_Growth_Var_tt = GNG_Base_Expected_Growth }
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = GNG_enabled_higher_growth_expectations
		}
		add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_Next_Year_Growth_Var_tt = 0.015 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_Base_Expected_Growth = 0.015 }
	}
	else = {
		add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_Next_Year_Growth_Var_tt = 0.01 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_Base_Expected_Growth = 0.01 }
	}
	every_owned_state = {
		set_temp_variable = { jap_app_temp = 2 }
		GNG_japanese_app_change = yes
		set_temp_variable = { zhu_app_temp = 1.5 }
		GNG_zhujin_app_change = yes
	}
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_approval_temp_var = 5 }
	GNG_Japan_approval_change = yes
	GNG_calculate_target_GDP = yes
	add_to_variable = { GNG_GDP_target_met_tracker = 1 }
	hidden_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_in_power = 4 }
			}
			add_to_variable = { GNG_GDP_matsushita_target_met_tracker = 1 }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { GNG_tokyo_meetings_counter = 6 } }
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { GNG_GDP_matsushita_target_met_tracker > 1 } }
					country_event = {
						id = guangdong_matsushitaflavor.58
						days = 15
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { GNG_GDP_matsushita_target_met_tracker < 2 } }
					country_event = {
						id = guangdong_matsushitaflavor.59
						days = 15
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

GNG_miss_GDP_target_effect = {
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_seat_temp = -3 }
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_temp = GNG_legco_faction_in_power }
	GNG_change_legco_seats = yes
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_Next_Year_Growth_Var_tt = GNG_Base_Expected_Growth }
	add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_Next_Year_Growth_Var_tt = -0.005 }
	add_to_variable = { GNG_Base_Expected_Growth = -0.005 }
	every_owned_state = {
		set_temp_variable = { jap_app_temp = -2 }
		GNG_japanese_app_change = yes
		set_temp_variable = { zhu_app_temp = -1.5 }
		GNG_zhujin_app_change = yes
	}
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_approval_temp_var = -5 }
	GNG_Japan_approval_change = yes
	GNG_calculate_target_GDP = yes
	hidden_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_in_power = 4 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { GNG_tokyo_meetings_counter = 6 } }
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { GNG_GDP_matsushita_target_met_tracker > 1 } }
					country_event = {
						id = guangdong_matsushitaflavor.58
						days = 15
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { GNG_GDP_matsushita_target_met_tracker < 2 } }
					country_event = {
						id = guangdong_matsushitaflavor.59
						days = 15
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

GNG_calculate_rGDP = {
	set_variable = { GNG_rGDP_debuff = this.modifier@GNG_rGDP_modifier }
	clamp_variable = {
		var = GNG_rGDP_debuff
		max = 0
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = TNO_has_started_up }
		update_economy_tab = yes
	}
}

GNG_calculate_fiscal_health = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				debt_to_GDP_ratio < 0.251
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { GNG_fiscal_status_var_temp = 0 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				debt_to_GDP_ratio < 0.501
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { GNG_fiscal_status_var_temp = 1 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				debt_to_GDP_ratio < 0.31
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { GNG_fiscal_status_var_temp = 2 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				debt_to_GDP_ratio < 1.001
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { GNG_fiscal_status_var_temp = 3 }
	}
	else = {
		set_temp_variable = { GNG_fiscal_status_var_temp = 4 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = GNG_disable_all_mechanics_IJA
			}
		}
		GNG_update_fiscal = yes
	}
}

GNG_yasuda_crisis_effects = {
	add_to_variable = { national_debt = 3.85 }
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = GNG_enabled_higher_debt
		}
		add_to_variable = { national_debt = 2.5 }
	}
	hidden_effect = {
		every_owned_state = {
			multiply_variable = {
				state_value = 0.88
			}
		}
	}
	custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_yasuda_crisis_economic_crisis
	subtract_from_variable = { gdp_growth = 2.5 }
	add_to_variable = { base_inflation_rate = 2.25 }
	calculate_debt_to_GDP_ratio = yes
	every_owned_state = {
		set_temp_variable = { jap_app_temp = -3 }
		GNG_japanese_app_change = yes
		set_temp_variable = { zhu_app_temp = -2 }
		GNG_zhujin_app_change = yes
		set_temp_variable = { chi_app_temp = -1 }
		GNG_chinese_app_change = yes
		set_temp_variable = { sar_spt_temp = -2.5 }
		GNG_police_control_change = yes
	}
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_general_status_var_temp = 1 }
	GNG_update_status = yes
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_security_status_var_temp = 5 }
	GNG_update_security = yes
	set_variable = { GNG_Base_Expected_Growth = 0.06 }
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = GNG_enabled_higher_growth_expectations
		}
		add_to_variable = { GNG_Base_Expected_Growth = 0.015 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = GNG_enabled_lower_growth_expectations
		}
		add_to_variable = { GNG_Base_Expected_Growth = -0.01 }
	}
	set_country_flag = yasuda_crisis
	mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
	recalculate_GDP_and_PUs_on_demand = yes
	calculate_debt_to_GDP_ratio = yes
	GNG_calculate_rGDP = yes
	update_economy_tab = yes
}

GNG_oil_crisis_effects = {
	add_to_variable = { national_debt = 1.75 }
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = GNG_enabled_higher_debt
		}
		add_to_variable = { national_debt = 2.5 }
	}
	custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_oil_crisis_economic_crisis
	clr_country_flag = GNG_desperate_economic_decisions_unlocked
	clr_country_flag = GNG_silicon_years_active
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = GNG_outraced_manchukuo
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_race_with_manchukuo_on_hold_OC_tt
	}
	subtract_from_variable = { gdp_growth = 5.5 }
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_in_power = 7 } #Hitachi
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { gdp_growth = 1 }
	}
	add_to_variable = { base_inflation_rate = 3 }
	set_variable = { GNG_Base_Expected_Growth = 0.05 }
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_in_power = 3 } #Sony
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = guangdong_commonOC.2
				days = 7
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				set_temp_variable = { jap_app_temp = -3 }
				GNG_japanese_app_change = yes
			}
			set_temp_variable = { GNG_approval_temp_var = -7.5 }
			GNG_Japan_approval_change = yes
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_japanese_empire_cap = -10 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_OC_sony_debuff
		load_focus_tree = GNG_morita_oil_crisis_tree
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_in_power = 4 } #Matsushita
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = guangdong_commonOC.3
				days = 7
			}
			set_temp_variable = { GNG_approval_temp_var = -7.5 }
			GNG_Japan_approval_change = yes
			set_temp_variable = { GNG_opinion_temp_var = -7.5 }
			GNG_China_opinion_change = yes
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_republic_of_china_cap = -5 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_japanese_empire_cap = -5 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_OC_matsushita_debuff
		load_focus_tree = GNG_matsushita_oil_crisis_tree
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_in_power = 5 } #Fujitsu
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = guangdong_commonOC.4
				days = 7
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				set_temp_variable = { chi_app_temp = -3 }
				GNG_chinese_app_change = yes
			}
			set_temp_variable = { GNG_opinion_temp_var = -7.5 }
			GNG_China_opinion_change = yes
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_republic_of_china_cap = -10 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_OC_fujitsu_debuff
		load_focus_tree = GNG_ibuka_oil_crisis_tree
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_in_power = 7 } #Hitachi
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = guangdong_hitachiOC.4
				days = 4
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				set_temp_variable = { chi_app_temp = -3 }
				GNG_chinese_app_change = yes
				set_temp_variable = { zhu_app_temp = -3 }
				GNG_zhujin_app_change = yes
			}
			set_temp_variable = { GNG_opinion_temp_var = -7.5 }
			GNG_China_opinion_change = yes
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_republic_of_china_cap = -10 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_OC_hitachi_debuff
		load_focus_tree = GNG_komai_oil_crisis_tree
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
	}
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_general_status_var_temp = 3 }
	GNG_update_status = yes
	set_country_flag = GNG_oil_crisis
	hidden_effect = {
		recalculate_GDP_and_PUs_on_demand = yes
		calculate_debt_to_GDP_ratio = yes
		GNG_calculate_rGDP = yes
		update_economy_tab = yes
		GNG_stall_ordinance = yes
	}
	GNG_product_cycle_var_calc = yes
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_political_power > 499.99
		}
		set_political_power = 500
	}
}

GNG_execute_morita_crisis_event = {
	custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_morita_personal_crisis_events
	hidden_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { GNG_Morita_Personal_Crisis_var = 1 } }
			country_event = {
				id = guangdong_sonyMoritaCrisis.1
				hours = 6
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { GNG_Morita_Personal_Crisis_var = 2 } }
			country_event = {
				id = guangdong_sonyMoritaCrisis.2
				hours = 6
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { GNG_Morita_Personal_Crisis_var = 3 } }
			country_event = {
				id = guangdong_sonyMoritaCrisis.3
				hours = 6
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { GNG_Morita_Personal_Crisis_var = 5 } }
			country_event = {
				id = guangdong_sonyMoritaCrisis.4
				hours = 6
			}
		}
	}
}

### RIOTS ###

GNG_initialize_riots = {
	custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_riots_begin_tt
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_general_status_var_temp = 4 }
	GNG_update_status = yes
	set_variable = { GNG_Base_Expected_Growth = 0.05 }
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				GNG_legco_faction_in_power = 3 #Sony
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_GFT_Strength = 45 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_CCL_Strength = 45 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_GFT_Radicalism = 25 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_CCL_Radicalism = 35 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_Despair = 15 }
		set_country_flag = { flag = GNG_riots_60_day_limiter value = 1 days = 60 }
		set_country_flag = { flag = GNG_riots_240_day_limiter value = 1 days = 240 }

		set_variable = { GNG_Riots_Strength_Tick_base = 3 }
		set_variable = { GNG_Riots_Radicalism_Tick_base = 2.5 }
		set_variable = { GNG_Riots_Despair_Tick_base = 3.5 }
		set_variable = { GNG_Riots_Japanese_Intervention_Tick_base = 3.5 }
		randomize_variable = {
			var = riot_growth_next
			distribution = uniform
			min = 1
			max = 4.49 #Oddly specific value is to make sure that 3.5 and 4 are more normal values
		}
		round_variable = riot_growth_next
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { riot_growth_next > 1 } } #This is to generate x.5 or x.0 values
			random_list = {
				1 = {

				}
				1 = {
					subtract_from_variable = { riot_growth_next = 0.5 }
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_Riots_Map_Changes_Triad_Ally_tt
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GNG_China_Opinion < 50 }
			}
			add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_GFT_Strength = 5 }
			add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_CCL_Strength = 5 }
			add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_GFT_Radicalism = 7.5 }
			add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_CCL_Radicalism = 7.5 }
			set_country_flag = GNG_Chinese_intervention
			custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_Chinese_intervention_active
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GNG_zhu_app < 50 }
			}
			add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_GFT_Strength = 10 }
			add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_GFT_Radicalism = 7.5 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_Zhujin_anger_GFT_strength_radicalism
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GNG_chi_app < 50 }
			}
			add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_CCL_Strength = 10 }
			add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_CCL_Radicalism = 7.5 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_Chinese_anger_CCL_strength_radicalism
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { total_national_zhu_pop_percent < 0.2 }
			}
			add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_CCL_Strength = 10 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_low_zhujin_pop_CCL_strength
		}
		set_variable = { GNG_Japan_Riots = 100 }
		subtract_from_variable = { GNG_Japan_Riots = GNG_Japan_Approval }
		divide_variable = { GNG_Japan_Riots = 2 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_Japanese_Frustration_tt
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GNG_jap_app < 65 }
			}
			add_to_variable = { GNG_Japan_Riots = 10 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_japan_anger_frustration_increase
		}
		load_focus_tree = GNG_morita_riots
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				GNG_legco_faction_in_power = 4 #Matsushita
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_GFT_Strength = 50 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_CCL_Strength = 50 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_GFT_Radicalism = 35 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_CCL_Radicalism = 45 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_Despair = 15 }

		set_variable = { GNG_Riots_Strength_Tick_base = 3.5 }
		set_variable = { GNG_Riots_Radicalism_Tick_base = 2.5 }
		set_variable = { GNG_Riots_Despair_Tick_base = 3.5 }
		set_variable = { GNG_Riots_Japanese_Intervention_Tick_base = 3 }
		randomize_variable = {
			var = riot_growth_next
			distribution = uniform
			min = 1
			max = 4.49 #Oddly specific value is to make sure that 3.5 and 4 are more normal values
		}
		round_variable = riot_growth_next
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { riot_growth_next > 1 } } #This is to generate x.5 or x.0 values
			random_list = {
				1 = {

				}
				1 = {
					subtract_from_variable = { riot_growth_next = 0.5 }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				GNG = {
					has_country_flag = GNG_matsushita_yakuza_ally
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_Riots_Map_Changes_Yakuza_Ally_tt
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				GNG = {
					has_country_flag = GNG_matsushita_triad_ally
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_Riots_Map_Changes_Triad_Ally_tt
		}
		else = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_Riots_Map_Changes_No_Ally_tt
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GNG_China_Opinion < 50 }
			}
			add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_GFT_Strength = 5 }
			add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_CCL_Strength = 5 }
			add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_GFT_Radicalism = 7.5 }
			add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_CCL_Radicalism = 7.5 }
			set_country_flag = GNG_Chinese_intervention
			custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_Chinese_intervention_active
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GNG_zhu_app < 50 }
			}
			add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_GFT_Strength = 10 }
			add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_GFT_Radicalism = 7.5 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_Zhujin_anger_GFT_strength_radicalism
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GNG_chi_app < 50 }
			}
			add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_CCL_Strength = 10 }
			add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_CCL_Radicalism = 7.5 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_Chinese_anger_CCL_strength_radicalism
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { total_national_zhu_pop_percent < 0.2 }
			}
			add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_CCL_Strength = 10 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_low_zhujin_pop_CCL_strength
		}
		set_variable = { GNG_Japan_Riots = 100 }
		subtract_from_variable = { GNG_Japan_Riots = GNG_Japan_Approval }
		divide_variable = { GNG_Japan_Riots = 2 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_Japanese_Frustration_tt
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GNG_jap_app < 65 }
			}
			add_to_variable = { GNG_Japan_Riots = 10 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_japan_anger_frustration_increase
		}
		load_focus_tree = GNG_matsushita_riots_tree
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				GNG_legco_faction_in_power = 5 #Fujitsu
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_GFT_Strength = 50 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_CCL_Strength = 55 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_GFT_Radicalism = 45 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_CCL_Radicalism = 55 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_Despair = 15 }

		set_variable = { GNG_Riots_Strength_Tick_base = 3.5 }
		set_variable = { GNG_Riots_Radicalism_Tick_base = 2.5 }
		set_variable = { GNG_Riots_Despair_Tick_base = 3.5 }
		set_variable = { GNG_Riots_Japanese_Intervention_Tick_base = 3 }
		randomize_variable = {
			var = riot_growth_next
			distribution = uniform
			min = 1
			max = 4.49 #Oddly specific value is to make sure that 3.5 and 4 are more normal values
		}
		round_variable = riot_growth_next

			limit = { check_variable = { riot_growth_next > 1 } } #This is to generate x.5 or x.0 values

		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { total_national_zhu_pop_percent < 0.2 }
			}
			add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_CCL_Strength = 10 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_low_zhujin_pop_CCL_strength
		}
		set_variable = { GNG_Japan_Riots = 100 }
		subtract_from_variable = { GNG_Japan_Riots = GNG_Japan_Approval }
		divide_variable = { GNG_Japan_Riots = 2 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_Japanese_Frustration_tt
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GNG_jap_app < 65 }
			}
			add_to_variable = { GNG_Japan_Riots = 10 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_japan_anger_frustration_increase
		}
		load_focus_tree = GNG_komai_riots_tree
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
	}
	custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_riots_begin_chinese_and_japanese_consulate_close_tt
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = GNG_enable_harder_riots
		}
		add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_GFT_Strength = 10 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_CCL_Strength = 10 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_GFT_Radicalism = 10 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_CCL_Radicalism = 10 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_Despair = 10 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_Japan_Riots = 10 }

		add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_Strength_Tick_base = 0.5 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_Radicalism_Tick_base = 0.5 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_Despair_Tick_base = 0.5 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_Japanese_Intervention_Tick_base = 0.5 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = GNG_enable_easier_riots
		}
		add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_GFT_Strength = -10 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_CCL_Strength = -10 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_GFT_Radicalism = -10 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_CCL_Radicalism = -10 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_Despair = -10 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_Japan_Riots = -10 }

		add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_Strength_Tick_base = -0.5 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_Radicalism_Tick_base = -0.5 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_Despair_Tick_base = -0.5 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_Japanese_Intervention_Tick_base = -0.5 }
	}
	hidden_effect = {
		set_country_flag = GNG_Riots_Show_GUI
		set_country_flag = GNG_Riots_Active
		if = {
			limit = {
				GNG = {
					is_ai = no
				}
			}
			activate_mission = GNG_the_situation_updates
		}
		set_variable = { GNG_selected_riot_group = 1 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_political_power > 399.99
			}
			set_political_power = 400
		}
	}
	hidden_effect = {
		country_event = {
			id = guangdong_commonRiots.0
			days = 1
		}
		country_event  = {
			id = guangdong_commonRiots.1001 # for updating likelyhood of terror events to fire
			days = 20
		}
	}

	hidden_effect = {
		GNG_initialize_riots_underworld = yes
		GNG_Riots_var_calc = yes
	}
}

GNG_Riots_GFT_Strength_Change = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = GNG_Dismantlement_GFT_OVER
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { amount = GNG_Riots_GFT_Strength_Temp }
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { GNG_Riots_GFT_Strength_Temp < 0 } }
			multiply_temp_variable = { amount = -1 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_Riots_GFT_Strength_decrease_tt
		}
		else = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_Riots_GFT_Strength_increase_tt
		}
		add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_GFT_Strength = GNG_Riots_GFT_Strength_Temp }
		GNG_Riots_var_calc = yes
	}
}

	set_variable = { GNG_Riots_Strength_Tick = GNG_Riots_Strength_Tick_base }
	set_variable = { GNG_Riots_Radicalism_Tick = GNG_Riots_Radicalism_Tick_base }
	set_variable = { GNG_Riots_Despair_Tick = GNG_Riots_Despair_Tick_base }
	set_variable = { GNG_Riots_Japanese_Intervention_Tick = GNG_Riots_Japanese_Intervention_Tick_base }
	add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_Strength_Tick = modifier@GNG_Riots_Strength_Tick_modifier }
	add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_Radicalism_Tick = modifier@GNG_Riots_Radicalism_Tick_modifier }
	add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_Despair_Tick = modifier@GNG_Riots_Despair_Tick_modifier }
	add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_Japanese_Intervention_Tick = modifier@GNG_Riots_Japanese_Intervention_Tick_modifier }
	clamp_variable = {
		var = GNG_Riots_Strength_Tick
		min = 0
	}
	clamp_variable = {
		var = GNG_Riots_Radicalism_Tick
		min = 0
	}
	clamp_variable = {
		var = GNG_Riots_Despair_Tick
		min = 0
	}
	clamp_variable = {
		var = GNG_Riots_Japanese_Intervention_Tick
		min = 0
	}
}

GNG_Riots_Strength_Total_Calc = {
	clamp_variable = {
		var = GNG_Riots_GFT_Strength
		min = 0
		max = 100
	}
	clamp_variable = {
		var = GNG_Riots_CCL_Strength
		min = 0
		max = 100
	}
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_Strength_Total_Temp = GNG_Riots_GFT_Strength }
	add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_Strength_Total_Temp = GNG_Riots_CCL_Strength }
	divide_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_Strength_Total_Temp = 2 }
	set_variable = { GNG_Riots_Strength_Total = GNG_Riots_Strength_Total_Temp }
}

GNG_Riots_Radicalism_Total_Calc = {
	clamp_variable = {
		var = GNG_Riots_GFT_Radicalism
		min = 0
		max = 100
	}
	clamp_variable = {
		var = GNG_Riots_CCL_Radicalism
		min = 0
		max = 100
	}
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_Radicalism_Total_Temp = GNG_Riots_GFT_Radicalism }
	add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_Radicalism_Total_Temp = GNG_Riots_CCL_Radicalism }
	divide_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_Radicalism_Total_Temp = 2 }
	set_variable = { GNG_Riots_Radicalism_Total = GNG_Riots_Radicalism_Total_Temp }
}

GNG_Riots_GFT_AVG_Calc = {
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_GFT_AVG_Calc_Temp = GNG_Riots_GFT_Strength }
	add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_GFT_AVG_Calc_Temp = GNG_Riots_GFT_Radicalism }
	set_variable = { GNG_Riots_GFT_AVG = GNG_Riots_GFT_AVG_Calc_Temp }
}

GNG_Riots_CCL_AVG_Calc = {
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_CCL_AVG_Calc_Temp = GNG_Riots_CCL_Strength }
	add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_CCL_AVG_Calc_Temp = GNG_Riots_CCL_Radicalism }
	set_variable = { GNG_Riots_CCL_AVG = GNG_Riots_CCL_AVG_Calc_Temp }
}

GNG_Riots_Despair_Calc = {
	clamp_variable = {
		var = GNG_Riots_Despair
		min = 0
		max = 100
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_Riots_Despair > 66 }
		}
		set_variable = { GNG_Riots_Japanese_Intervention_Tick = 1 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_Riots_Despair > 33 }
		}
		set_variable = { GNG_Riots_Japanese_Intervention_Tick = 0.5 }
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { GNG_Riots_Japanese_Intervention_Tick = 0 }
	}
}

GNG_Japan_Riots_Calc = {
	clamp_variable = {
		var = GNG_Japan_Riots
		min = 0
		max = 100
	}
}

GNG_fire_riots_event = {
	random_list = { # should a protestor or police event fire
		var:GNG_riot_event_chance = { # set in guangdong_commonRiots.1001
			GNG_riots_fire_terror_event = yes
		}
		1 = {
			GNG_riots_fire_police_event = yes
		}
	}
	random_list = { # sets the target group for the upcoming event. Would use random lists in the events but the tooltip doesn't look nice
		1 = {
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = GNG_Dismantlement_GFT_OVER
			}
			set_variable = { GNG_riot_event_target = 0 }
		}
		1 = {
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = GNG_Dismantlement_CCL_OVER
			}
			set_variable = { GNG_riot_event_target = 1 }
		}
	}
}

GNG_riots_fire_terror_event = {
	if = { # has terror flag
		limit = { has_country_flag = GNG_riots_terror_active }
		random_list = {
			1 = {
				country_event = { id = guangdong_commonRiots.128 hours = 6 }
			}
			1 = {
				country_event = { id = guangdong_commonRiots.129 hours = 6 }
			}
			1 = {
				country_event = { id = guangdong_commonRiots.130 hours = 6 }
			}
			1 = {
				country_event = { id = guangdong_commonRiots.131 hours = 6 }
			}
			1 = {
				country_event = { id = guangdong_commonRiots.132 hours = 6 }
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = { # low radicalism
		limit = { check_variable = { GNG_Riots_Radicalism_Total < 33 } }
		random_list = {
			1 = {
				country_event = { id = guangdong_commonRiots.100 hours = 6 }
			}
			1 = {
				country_event = { id = guangdong_commonRiots.101 hours = 6 }
			}
			1 = {
				country_event = { id = guangdong_commonRiots.102 hours = 6 }
			}
			1 = {
				country_event = { id = guangdong_commonRiots.103 hours = 6 }
			}
			1 = {
				country_event = { id = guangdong_commonRiots.104 hours = 6 }
			}
			1 = {
				country_event = { id = guangdong_commonRiots.105 hours = 6 }
			}
			1 = {
				country_event = { id = guangdong_commonRiots.106 hours = 6 }
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = { # high radicalism
		limit = { check_variable = { GNG_Riots_Radicalism_Total > 66 } }
		random_list = {
			1 = {
				country_event = { id = guangdong_commonRiots.118 hours = 6 }
			}
			1 = {
				country_event = { id = guangdong_commonRiots.119 hours = 6 }
			}
			1 = {
				country_event = { id = guangdong_commonRiots.120 hours = 6 }
			}
			1 = {
				country_event = { id = guangdong_commonRiots.121 hours = 6 }
			}
			1 = {
				country_event = { id = guangdong_commonRiots.122 hours = 6 }
			}
			1 = {
				country_event = { id = guangdong_commonRiots.123 hours = 6 }
			}
			1 = {
				country_event = { id = guangdong_commonRiots.124 hours = 6 }
			}
		}
	}
	else = { # med radicalism
		random_list = {
			1 = {
				country_event = { id = guangdong_commonRiots.109 hours = 6 }
			}
			1 = {
				country_event = { id = guangdong_commonRiots.110 hours = 6 }
			}
			1 = {
				country_event = { id = guangdong_commonRiots.111 hours = 6 }
			}
			1 = {
				country_event = { id = guangdong_commonRiots.112 hours = 6 }
			}
			1 = {
				country_event = { id = guangdong_commonRiots.113 hours = 6 }
			}
			1 = {
				country_event = { id = guangdong_commonRiots.114 hours = 6 }
			}
			1 = {
				country_event = { id = guangdong_commonRiots.115 hours = 6 }
			}
		}
	}
}

GNG_riots_police_event_effects = {
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_Despair_Temp = -3 }
	GNG_Despair_Change = yes
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { GNG_riot_event_target = 0 } }
		set_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_GFT_Strength_Temp = -3 }
		GNG_Riots_GFT_Strength_Change = yes
		set_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_GFT_Radicalism_Temp = -1.5 }
		GNG_Riots_GFT_Radicalism_Change = yes
	}
	else = {
		set_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_CCL_Strength_Temp = -3 }
		GNG_Riots_CCL_Strength_Change = yes
		set_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_CCL_Radicalism_Temp = -1.5 }
		GNG_Riots_CCL_Radicalism_Change = yes
	}
	random_owned_state = {
		set_temp_variable = { govt_spt_temp = 2 }
		GNG_government_control_change = yes
	}
	random_owned_state = {
		set_temp_variable = { govt_spt_temp = 2 }
		GNG_government_control_change = yes
	}
	clear_variable = GNG_riot_event_target
}

GNG_riots_event_effects_low_rad = {

		set_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_GFT_Strength_Temp = 1.5 }
		GNG_Riots_GFT_Strength_Change = yes
	}
	else = {

		set_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_CCL_Strength_Temp = 1.5 }
		GNG_Riots_CCL_Strength_Change = yes
	}
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_Japan_Riots_Temp = 2 }
	GNG_Japanese_Intervention_Change = yes
	random_owned_state = {
		set_temp_variable = { riot_spt_temp = 1 }
		GNG_rioters_control_change = yes
	}
	random_owned_state = {
		set_temp_variable = { riot_spt_temp = 1 }
		GNG_rioters_control_change = yes

	clear_variable = GNG_riot_event_target
}

GNG_Riots_Ending = {
	#Fires after guangdong_commonRiots.9 event, switches focus trees to the ending
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_in_power = 3 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = GNG_morita_personal_crisis_good_end
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				GNG_morita_akio = {
					set_portraits = {
						civilian = { large = "gfx/leaders/GNG/GNG_Morita_Akio_70s.dds" }
					}
				}
				set_country_leader_description = {
					desc = "POLITICS_MORITA_AKIO_70S_DESC"
				}
				remove_trait = {
					character = GNG_morita_akio
					trait = the_gadgeteer_of_guangdong
					ideology = paternalism_corporate_paternalism_subtype
				}
				add_trait = {
					character = GNG_morita_akio
					trait = custodian_of_a_dream
					ideology = paternalism_corporate_paternalism_subtype
				}
				GNG_li_kashing = {
					set_portraits = {
						civilian = { small = "GFX_idea_GNG_minister_Li_Ka_Shing_70s_success" }
					}
					remove_advisor_role = { slot = head_of_government }
					add_advisor_role = {
						advisor = {
							slot = head_of_government
							idea_token = GNG_li_kashing_70s_1_hog
							traits = {
								head_of_government
								hog_the_co_custodian
							}
							ledger = civilian
							cost = -1
						}
					}
				}
				GNG_matsushita_masaharu = {
					set_portraits = {
						civilian = { small = "GFX_idea_GNG_minister_Matsushita_Masaharu_70s" }
					}
					remove_advisor_role = { slot = foreign_minister }
					add_advisor_role = {
						advisor = {
							slot = foreign_minister
							idea_token = GNG_matsushita_morita_70s_1_for
							traits = {
								foreign_minister
								for_to_endeavors_ahead
							}
							ledger = civilian
							cost = -1
						}
					}
				}
				add_ideas = {
					GNG_li_kashing_70s_1_hog
					GNG_matsushita_morita_70s_1_for
				}
				set_country_flag = GNG_morita_personal_victory_achievement
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_morita_personal_crisis_good_end_riots_end_tt
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = GNG_morita_personal_crisis_bad_end
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				GNG_morita_akio = {
					set_portraits = {
						civilian = { large = "gfx/leaders/GNG/GNG_Morita_Akio_70s_failure.dds" }
					}
				}
				set_country_leader_description = {
					desc = "POLITICS_MORITA_AKIO_70S_FAILURE_DESC"
				}
				remove_trait = {
					character = GNG_morita_akio
					trait = the_gadgeteer_of_guangdong
					ideology = paternalism_corporate_paternalism_subtype
				}
				add_trait = {
					character = GNG_morita_akio
					trait = president_of_sony
					ideology = paternalism_corporate_paternalism_subtype
				}
				GNG_li_kashing = {
					set_portraits = {
						civilian = { small = "GFX_idea_GNG_minister_Li_Ka_Shing_70s_success" }
					}
					remove_advisor_role = { slot = head_of_government }
					add_advisor_role = {
						advisor = {
							slot = head_of_government
							idea_token = GNG_li_kashing_70s_1_hog
							traits = {
								head_of_government
								hog_the_co_custodian
							}
							ledger = civilian
							cost = -1
						}
					}
				}
				GNG_matsushita_masaharu = {
					set_portraits = {
						civilian = { small = "GFX_idea_GNG_minister_Matsushita_Masaharu_70s" }
					}
					remove_advisor_role = { slot = foreign_minister }
					add_advisor_role = {
						advisor = {
							slot = foreign_minister
							idea_token = GNG_matsushita_morita_70s_2_for
							traits = {
								foreign_minister
								for_another_poisoned_chalice

							ledger = civilian
							cost = -1

					}
				}

GNG_Arms_Market_Product_Select = {
	set_variable = { GNG_arms_market_active_price = GNG_arms_market_price_list^GNG_arms_market_product_selected }
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { GNG_arms_market_country_selected = 0 } }
		multiply_variable = { GNG_arms_market_active_price = GNG_Arms_Market_Japan_Sales_Multiplier^GNG_arms_market_product_selected }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { GNG_arms_market_country_selected = 1 } }
		multiply_variable = { GNG_arms_market_active_price = GNG_Arms_Market_China_Sales_Multiplier^GNG_arms_market_product_selected }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { GNG_arms_market_country_selected = 2 } }
		multiply_variable = { GNG_arms_market_active_price = GNG_Arms_Market_Indonesia_Sales_Multiplier^GNG_arms_market_product_selected }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { GNG_arms_market_country_selected = 3 } }
		multiply_variable = { GNG_arms_market_active_price = GNG_Arms_Market_Free_Indonesia_Sales_Multiplier^GNG_arms_market_product_selected }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { GNG_arms_market_country_selected = 4 } }
		multiply_variable = { GNG_arms_market_active_price = GNG_Arms_Market_Thailand_Sales_Multiplier^GNG_arms_market_product_selected }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { GNG_arms_market_country_selected = 5 } }
		multiply_variable = { GNG_arms_market_active_price = GNG_Arms_Market_Azad_Hind_Sales_Multiplier^GNG_arms_market_product_selected }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { GNG_arms_market_country_selected = 6 } }
		multiply_variable = { GNG_arms_market_active_price = GNG_Arms_Market_Shonan_Sales_Multiplier^GNG_arms_market_product_selected }
	}
	set_variable = { GNG_arms_market_active_price_mil = GNG_arms_market_active_price }
	multiply_variable = { GNG_arms_market_active_price_mil = 1000 }

	set_variable = { GNG_arms_market_product_quantity = GNG_arms_market_quantity_list^GNG_arms_market_product_selected }

	set_variable = { GNG_arms_market_product_activity = GNG_arms_market_activity_list^GNG_arms_market_product_selected }

	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { GNG_arms_market_activity_list^GNG_arms_market_product_selected > GNG_arms_market_total_activity } }
		set_variable = { GNG_arms_market_option_button = 1 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			set_temp_variable = { GNG_arms_market_id_temp = GNG_arms_market_product_tech_list^GNG_arms_market_product_selected }
			check_variable = { num_equipment@var:GNG_arms_market_id_temp < GNG_arms_market_quantity_list^GNG_arms_market_product_selected }
		}
		set_variable = { GNG_arms_market_option_button = 2 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { GNG_Arms_Market_Country_Money_List^GNG_arms_market_country_selected < GNG_arms_market_price_list^GNG_arms_market_product_selected } }
		set_variable = { GNG_arms_market_option_button = 3 }
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { GNG_arms_market_option_button = 4 }
	}
}

GNG_Arms_Market_Sell_Product = {
	set_temp_variable = { money_reserves_temp = GNG_arms_market_active_price }
	econ_money_reserves_change_raw_money = yes
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_Arms_Market_Sales_Temp = GNG_arms_market_product_tech_list^GNG_arms_market_product_selected }
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_arms_Market_eq_loss_temp = GNG_arms_market_quantity_list^GNG_arms_market_product_selected }
	multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_arms_Market_eq_loss_temp = -1 }
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_arms_Market_eq_gain_temp = GNG_arms_market_quantity_list^GNG_arms_market_product_selected }

	GNG = {
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = var:GNG_Arms_Market_Sales_Temp
			amount = GNG_arms_Market_eq_loss_temp
			producer = GNG
		}
	}

	set_variable = { GNG_Arms_Market_Target_Var = GNG_Arms_Market_Country_Scope_List^GNG_arms_market_country_selected }


	var:GNG_Arms_Market_Target_Var = {
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = var:GNG.GNG_Arms_Market_Sales_Temp
			amount = GNG.GNG_arms_Market_eq_gain_temp
			producer = GNG
		}
	}

	subtract_from_variable = { GNG_arms_market_total_activity = GNG_arms_market_activity_list^GNG_arms_market_product_selected }
	subtract_from_variable = { GNG_Arms_Market_Country_Money_List^GNG_arms_market_country_selected = GNG_arms_market_active_price }

	GNG_Arms_Market_Product_Select = yes
}

GNG_Arms_Market_Yearly_Refresh = {
	set_variable = { GNG_arms_market_total_activity = 100 }
	set_variable = { GNG_Arms_Market_Country_Money_List^0 = 1 }
	set_variable = { GNG_Arms_Market_Country_Money_List^1 = 0.6 }
	set_variable = { GNG_Arms_Market_Country_Money_List^2 = 0.4 }
	set_variable = { GNG_Arms_Market_Country_Money_List^3 = 0.4 }
	set_variable = { GNG_Arms_Market_Country_Money_List^4 = 0.3 }
	set_variable = { GNG_Arms_Market_Country_Money_List^5 = 0.3 }
	set_variable = { GNG_Arms_Market_Country_Money_List^6 = 0.15 }
}

GNG_ibuka_trademark_passed_support = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = GNG_the_guangdong_trademark_ordinance_passed
		}
		add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_sony_temp_support = -0.2 } #1 = 100%
		add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_cheungkong_temp_support = -0.2 } #1 = 100%
	}
}

GNG_ibuka_anti_corruption_passed_support = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = GNG_ibuka_anti_corruption_passed
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = GNG_ibuka_anti_corruption_2_passed
				}
			}
		}
		add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_sony_temp_support = 0.05 } #1 = 100%
		add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_matsushita_temp_support = 0.1 } #1 = 100%
		add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_cheungkong_temp_support = 0.05 } #1 = 100%
		add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_temp_votes_percentage = 0.1 } #1 = 100%
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = GNG_ibuka_anti_corruption_2_passed
		}
		add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_sony_temp_support = -0.1 } #1 = 100%
		add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_matsushita_temp_support = 0.1 } #1 = 100%
		add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_cheungkong_temp_support = -0.1 } #1 = 100%
		add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_hitachi_temp_support = 0.1 } #1 = 100%
	}
}

GNG_ibuka_modern_police_passed_support = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = GNG_ibuka_modern_police_1_passed
		}
		add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_hitachi_temp_support = -0.2 } #1 = 100%
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = GNG_ibuka_modern_police_2_passed
		}
		add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_hitachi_temp_support = 0.2 } #1 = 100%
	}
}

GNG_test = {
	randomize_variable = {
		var = riot_growth_next
		distribution = uniform
		min = 1
		max = 4.49
	}
	round_variable = riot_growth_next
	hidden_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { riot_growth_next > 1 }
			} #This is to generate x.5 or x.0 values
			random_list = {
				1 = {

				}
				1 = {
					subtract_from_variable = { riot_growth_next = 0.5 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

## PROPOSALS STUFF ###

GNG_Proposals_Popup_Open = {
	clear_array = GNG_Proposals_Array
	for_loop_effect = {
		start = 1
		end = 11
		value = v
		add_to_array = { GNG_Proposals_Array = v }
	}
	set_variable = { GNG_Proposals_Current_Selected_Proposal = 0 }
	set_country_flag = GNG_Negotiations_Proposals_Visible
}

GNG_negotiations_add_seats = {
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_fujitsu_check = GNG_legco_fujitsu_seats }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_fujitsu_check = GNG_legco_faction_support^5 }
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_matsushita_check = GNG_legco_matsushita_seats }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_matsushita_check = GNG_legco_faction_support^4 }
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_sony_check = GNG_legco_sony_seats }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_sony_check = GNG_legco_faction_support^3 }
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_cheung_kong_check = GNG_legco_cheungkong_seats }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_cheung_kong_check = GNG_legco_faction_support^6 }
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_hitachi_check = GNG_legco_hitachi_seats }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_hitachi_check = GNG_legco_faction_support^7 }
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_in_power = 3 } #Sony
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GNG_legco_sony_check < GNG_votes_needed }
			}
			add_to_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_support^3 = GNG_legco_sony_check }
			subtract_from_variable = { GNG_votes_needed = GNG_legco_sony_check }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { GNG_legco_cheung_kong_check < GNG_votes_needed }
				}
				add_to_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_support^6 = GNG_legco_cheung_kong_check }
				subtract_from_variable = { GNG_votes_needed = GNG_legco_cheung_kong_check }
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { GNG_legco_matsushita_check < GNG_votes_needed }
					}
					add_to_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_support^4 = GNG_legco_matsushita_check }
					subtract_from_variable = { GNG_votes_needed = GNG_legco_matsushita_check }
					if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { GNG_legco_fujitsu_check < GNG_votes_needed }
						}
						add_to_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_support^5 = GNG_legco_fujitsu_check }
						subtract_from_variable = { GNG_votes_needed = GNG_legco_fujitsu_check }
						add_to_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_support^7 = GNG_votes_needed }
					}
					else = {
						add_to_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_support^5 = GNG_votes_needed }
					}
				}
				else = {
					add_to_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_support^4 = GNG_votes_needed }
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_to_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_support^6 = GNG_votes_needed }
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_to_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_support^3 = GNG_votes_needed }
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_in_power = 4 } #Matsushita
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GNG_legco_matsushita_check < GNG_votes_needed }
			}
			add_to_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_support^4 = GNG_legco_matsushita_check }
			subtract_from_variable = { GNG_votes_needed = GNG_legco_matsushita_check }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { GNG_legco_cheung_kong_check < GNG_votes_needed }
				}
				add_to_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_support^6 = GNG_legco_cheung_kong_check }
				subtract_from_variable = { GNG_votes_needed = GNG_legco_cheung_kong_check }
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { GNG_legco_sony_check < GNG_votes_needed }
					}
					add_to_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_support^3 = GNG_legco_sony_check }
					subtract_from_variable = { GNG_votes_needed = GNG_legco_sony_check }
					if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { GNG_legco_fujitsu_check < GNG_votes_needed }
						}
						add_to_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_support^5 = GNG_legco_fujitsu_check }
						subtract_from_variable = { GNG_votes_needed = GNG_legco_fujitsu_check }
						add_to_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_support^7 = GNG_votes_needed }
					}
					else = {
						add_to_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_support^5 = GNG_votes_needed }
					}
				}
				else = {
					add_to_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_support^3 = GNG_votes_needed }
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_to_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_support^6 = GNG_votes_needed }
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_to_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_support^4 = GNG_votes_needed }
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_in_power = 5 } #Fujitsu
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GNG_legco_fujitsu_check < GNG_votes_needed }
			}
			add_to_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_support^5 = GNG_legco_fujitsu_check }
			subtract_from_variable = { GNG_votes_needed = GNG_legco_fujitsu_check }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { GNG_legco_cheung_kong_check < GNG_votes_needed }
				}
				add_to_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_support^6 = GNG_legco_cheung_kong_check }
				subtract_from_variable = { GNG_votes_needed = GNG_legco_cheung_kong_check }
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { GNG_legco_sony_check < GNG_votes_needed }
					}
					add_to_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_support^3 = GNG_legco_sony_check }
					subtract_from_variable = { GNG_votes_needed = GNG_legco_sony_check }
					if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { GNG_legco_matsushita_check < GNG_votes_needed }
						}
						add_to_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_support^4 = GNG_legco_matsushita_check }
						subtract_from_variable = { GNG_votes_needed = GNG_legco_matsushita_check }
						add_to_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_support^7 = GNG_votes_needed }
					}
					else = {
						add_to_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_support^4 = GNG_votes_needed }
					}
				}
				else = {
					add_to_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_support^3 = GNG_votes_needed }
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_to_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_support^6 = GNG_votes_needed }
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_to_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_support^5 = GNG_votes_needed }
		}
	}
	set_variable = { GNG_votes_needed = 0 }
	GNG_check_votes_legco = yes
}

GNG_IJA_piechart_manipulation = {
	set_temp_variable = { party_pop_multiplier = 1 }
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_IJA_takeover_party_pop_calc = GNG_IJA_takeover_party_pop }
	divide_temp_variable = { GNG_IJA_takeover_party_pop_calc = 100 }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { party_pop_multiplier = GNG_IJA_takeover_party_pop_calc }

	set_temp_variable = { GNG_IJA_paternalism_holding_calc = GNG_IJA_paternalism_holding }
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_IJA_paternalism_2_holding_calc = GNG_IJA_paternalism_2_holding }
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_IJA_despotism_holding_calc = GNG_IJA_despotism_holding }
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_IJA_despotism_1_holding_calc = GNG_IJA_despotism_1_holding }
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_IJA_despotism_2_holding_calc = GNG_IJA_despotism_2_holding }
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_IJA_fascism_holding_calc = GNG_IJA_fascism_holding }
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_IJA_fascism_3_holding_calc = GNG_IJA_fascism_3_holding }
	multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_IJA_paternalism_holding_calc = party_pop_multiplier }
	multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_IJA_paternalism_2_holding_calc = party_pop_multiplier }
	multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_IJA_despotism_holding_calc = party_pop_multiplier }
	multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_IJA_despotism_1_holding_calc = party_pop_multiplier }
	multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_IJA_despotism_2_holding_calc = party_pop_multiplier }
	multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_IJA_fascism_holding_calc = party_pop_multiplier }
	multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_IJA_fascism_3_holding_calc = party_pop_multiplier }
	multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_IJA_paternalism_holding_calc = 100 }
	multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_IJA_paternalism_2_holding_calc = 100 }
	multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_IJA_despotism_holding_calc = 100 }
	multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_IJA_despotism_1_holding_calc = 100 }
	multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_IJA_despotism_2_holding_calc = 100 }
	multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_IJA_fascism_holding_calc = 100 }
	multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_IJA_fascism_3_holding_calc = 100 }

	set_popularities = {
		paternalism = var:GNG_IJA_paternalism_holding_calc
		paternalism_2 = var:GNG_IJA_paternalism_2_holding_calc
		despotism = var:GNG_IJA_despotism_holding_calc
		despotism_1 = var:GNG_IJA_despotism_1_holding_calc
		despotism_2 = var:GNG_IJA_despotism_2_holding_calc
		fascism = var:GNG_IJA_fascism_holding_calc
		fascism_3 = var:GNG_IJA_fascism_3_holding_calc
		ultranationalism = var:GNG_IJA_takeover_party_pop
	}
}

					id = guangdong_IJAFailstate.22
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_in_power_holding = 7 }
				}
				country_event = {
					id = guangdong_IJAFailstate.23
				}
			}
			activate_mission = GNG_the_wheel_turns
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = GNG_the_wheel_turns
				days = -5
			}
			set_temp_variable = { v = 10 }
			GNG_IJA_add_takeover_progress = yes
			add_to_variable = { GNG_IJA_takeover_party_pop = 10 }
			GNG_IJA_piechart_manipulation = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GNG_IJA_wheel_turns_counter = 8 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_in_power_holding = 3 }
				}
				country_event = {
					id = guangdong_IJAFailstate.25
				}
			}
			else = {
				country_event = {
					id = guangdong_IJAFailstate.26
				}
			}
			activate_mission = GNG_the_wheel_turns
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = GNG_the_wheel_turns
				days = -5
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GNG_IJA_wheel_turns_counter = 9 }
			}
			country_event = {
				id = guangdong_IJAFailstate.24
			}
			activate_mission = GNG_the_wheel_turns
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = GNG_the_wheel_turns
				days = -5
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GNG_IJA_wheel_turns_counter = 10 }
			}
			country_event = {
				id = guangdong_IJAFailstate.29
			}
			activate_mission = GNG_the_wheel_turns
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = GNG_the_wheel_turns
				days = -5
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GNG_IJA_wheel_turns_counter = 11 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_in_power_holding = 7 }
				}
				country_event = {
					id = guangdong_IJAFailstate.32
				}
			}
			else = {
				country_event = {
					id = guangdong_IJAFailstate.31
				}
			}
			activate_mission = GNG_the_wheel_turns
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = GNG_the_wheel_turns
				days = -5
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GNG_IJA_wheel_turns_counter = 12 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_in_power_holding = 7 }
				}
				country_event = {
					id = guangdong_IJAFailstate.28
				}
			}
			else = {
				country_event = {
					id = guangdong_IJAFailstate.27
				}
			}
			remove_mission = GNG_the_wheel_turns
		}
	}
}

GNG_IJA_add_takeover_progress = {
	add_to_variable = { GNG_IJA_takeover_progress = v }
	clamp_variable = { var = GNG_IJA_takeover_progress min = 0 max = 100 }

	set_variable = { GNG_IJA_bar_x = GNG_IJA_takeover_progress }
	divide_variable = { GNG_IJA_bar_x = 100 }
	multiply_variable = { GNG_IJA_bar_x = 491 }
	add_to_variable = { GNG_IJA_bar_x = -8 }
	clamp_variable = { var = GNG_IJA_bar_x min = 8 max = 464 }

}

GNG_IJA_remove_takeover_progress = {
	add_to_variable = { GNG_IJA_takeover_progress = v }
	clamp_variable = { var = GNG_IJA_takeover_progress min = 0 max = 100 }

	set_variable = { GNG_IJA_bar_x = GNG_IJA_takeover_progress }
	divide_variable = { GNG_IJA_bar_x = 100 }
	multiply_variable = { GNG_IJA_bar_x = 491 }
	add_to_variable = { GNG_IJA_bar_x = -8 }
	clamp_variable = { var = GNG_IJA_bar_x min = 8 max = 464 }
}
